# Repetition Algorithms - Obsidian Spaced Repetition

 

[Skip to content](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/algorithms/#learning-algorithms)

Learning Algorithms[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/algorithms/#learning-algorithms "Permanent link")

==============================================================================================================================

A learning algorithm is a formula that determines when a note or flashcard should next be reviewed.

| Algorithm | Status |
| --- | --- |
| [SM-2-OSR](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/algorithms/#sm-2-osr) | Implemented |
| [FSRS](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/algorithms/#fsrs) | Planned |
| [User Defined Intervals](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/algorithms/#user-specified-intervals) | Planned |

SM-2-OSR[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/algorithms/#sm-2-osr "Permanent link")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   The `SM-2-OSR` algorithm is a variant of [Anki's algorithm](https://faqs.ankiweb.net/what-spaced-repetition-algorithm.html)
     which is based on the [SM-2 algorithm](https://www.supermemo.com/en/archives1990-2015/english/ol/sm2)
    .
*   It supports ternary reviews i.e. a concept is either hard, good, or easy at the time of review.
*   initial ease is weighted (using max\_link\_factor) depending on the average ease of linked notes, note importance, and the base ease.
*   Anki also applies a small amount of random “fuzz” to prevent cards that were introduced at the same time and given the same ratings from sticking together and always coming up for review on the same day.
*   The algorithm is essentially the same for both notes and flashcards - apart from the PageRanks

### Algorithm Details[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/algorithms/#algorithm-details "Permanent link")

Warning

Note that this hasn't been updated in a while, please see the [code](https://github.com/st3v3nmw/obsidian-spaced-repetition/blob/master/src/algorithms/osr/srs-algorithm-osr.ts)
.

*   `if link_count > 0: initial_ease = (1 - link_contribution) * base_ease + link_contribution * average_ease` - `link_contribution = max_link_factor * min(1.0, log(link_count + 0.5) / log(64))` (cater for uncertainty)
    *   The importance of the different concepts/notes is determined using the PageRank algorithm (not all notes are created equal xD)
        *   On most occasions, the most fundamental concepts/notes have higher importance
*   If the user reviews a concept/note as:
    *   easy, the ease increases by `20` and the interval changes to `old_interval * new_ease / 100 * 1.3` (the 1.3 is the easy bonus)
    *   good, the ease remains unchanged and the interval changes to `old_interval * old_ease / 100`
    *   hard, the ease decreases by `20` and the interval changes to `old_interval * 0.5`
        *   The `0.5` can be modified in settings
        *   `minimum ease = 130`
    *   For `8` or more days:
        *   `interval += random_choice({-fuzz, 0, +fuzz})`
            *   where `fuzz = ceil(0.05 * interval)`
            *   [Anki docs](https://faqs.ankiweb.net/what-spaced-repetition-algorithm.html)
                : > "\[...\] Anki also applies a small amount of random “fuzz” to prevent cards that were introduced at the same time and given the same ratings from sticking together and always coming up for review on the same day."
*   The scheduling information is stored in the YAML front matter

* * *

FSRS[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/algorithms/#fsrs "Permanent link")

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The algorithm is detailed at: [fsrs4anki](https://github.com/open-spaced-repetition/fsrs4anki/wiki)

Incorporation of the FSRS algorithm into this plugin has not yet occurred. For progress see: [\[FEAT\] sm-2 is outdated, can you please replace it with the fsrs algorithm? #748](https://github.com/st3v3nmw/obsidian-spaced-repetition/issues/748)

* * *

User Specified Intervals[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/algorithms/#user-specified-intervals "Permanent link")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This is the simplest "algorithm" possible. There are fixed intervals configured by the user for each of the possible review outcomes.

For example, `hard` might be configured for an interval of 1 day.

Implementation of this technique has not yet occurred. For progress see: [\[FEAT\] user defined "Easy, Good, Hard" values instead of or in addition to the algorithm defined one. #741](https://github.com/st3v3nmw/obsidian-spaced-repetition/issues/741)

Back to top

---

# Data Storage - Obsidian Spaced Repetition

 

[Skip to content](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/data-storage/#data-storage)

Data Storage[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/data-storage/#data-storage "Permanent link")

==================================================================================================================

Scheduling Information[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/data-storage/#scheduling-information "Permanent link")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### Individual Markdown Files[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/data-storage/#individual-markdown-files "Permanent link")

This is the original method used for storing the scheduling information for cards and notes.

For cards this is stored in an HTML comment for that card. For example with the card:

`[](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/data-storage/#__codelineno-0-1) The RCU and WCU limits for a single partition key value::3000 RCU, 1000 WCU`

When the card is reviewed, an HTML comment will be added after the card's text, such as:

`[](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/data-storage/#__codelineno-1-1) <!--SR:!2024-08-16,51,230-->`

By default, the comment is stored on the line following the card text. Alternatively, it can be stored on the same line by enabling the [Save scheduling comment on the same line as the flashcard's last line?](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/user-options/#storage-of-scheduling-data)
 option.

Scheduling information for the note is kept at the beginning of the file, in YAML format within the frontmatter section. For example:

![note-frontmatter](https://github.com/user-attachments/assets/b9744f50-c897-46ad-ab34-1bbc55796b57)

Raw text format

* * *

sr-due: 2024-07-01 sr-interval: 3 sr-ease: 269

* * *

### Single Scheduling File[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/data-storage/#single-scheduling-file "Permanent link")

The scheduling information for all cards and notes is kept in a single dedicated file.

Implementation of this has not yet occurred. For progress see:

[\[FEAT\] Stop using YAML; Move plugin info and data to separate file #162](https://github.com/st3v3nmw/obsidian-spaced-repetition/issues/162)

* * *

User Options[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/data-storage/#user-options "Permanent link")

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

All user [options](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/user-options/)
 are stored in `data.json` in the plugin folder.

* * *

Card Postponement List[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/data-storage/#card-postponement-list "Permanent link")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This records a list of cards reviewed today that have sibling cards that shouldn't be reviewed until tomorrow.

Cards are only added to this list if the [Bury sibling cards until the next day](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/user-options/#flashcard-review)
 setting is turned on.

This information is also kept in the `data.json` file.

Note

To minimise the space required for this, a copy of the card is not stored. Rather a small numeric hash code ("fingerprint") is kept.

Back to top

---

# Notes - Obsidian Spaced Repetition

 

[Skip to content](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/notes/#notes)

Notes[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/notes/#notes "Permanent link")

=============================================================================================

Tip

For guidelines on how to write and structure notes, see [Spaced Repetition Guides](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/resources/#notes)

Getting started[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/notes/#getting-started "Permanent link")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Tag any markdown files for review with the `note review` tag, which by default is `#review`.

The note will appear under `New` in the `Note Review Queue` in the right pane.

Note

When you tag a note with `#review` the note doesn't immediately appear in the review queue. You will need to first click on the `Flashcard Review Icon` or the `Spaced Repetition Status Area` for the queue to update

Note Review Queue[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/notes/#note-review-queue "Permanent link")

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![note-review-queue](https://github.com/user-attachments/assets/c0e1d09c-610f-4775-b532-ab78369b117a)

1.  The Note Review Queue  
    
2.  The `Note Review Deck` for tag `#review`  
    
3.  The new notes - i.e. those tagged with `#review` but have yet to be reviewed  
    
4.  The notes scheduled for review on August 1  
    
5.  The notes scheduled for review on August 31  
    

### Displaying the Note Review Queue[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/notes/#displaying-the-note-review-queue "Permanent link")

By default, the Note Review Queue is displayed when the plugin starts. This can be changed with the `Enable note review pane on startup` [setting](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/user-options/#note-settings)
.

The Note Review Queue can also be shown by using the `Open Notes Review Queue in sidebar` [command](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/plugin-commands/)
.

Reviewing[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/notes/#reviewing "Permanent link")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Open a file, read & review it. Once done, choose either the `Review: Easy`, `Review: Good`, or the `Review: Hard` option on the file menu (the three dots). Select `Easy`, `Good`, or `Hard` depend on how well you comprehend the material being reviewed.

![file-three-dots-menu](https://github.com/user-attachments/assets/5f37ab88-30f9-477d-b39c-eb86ba15abdb)

Alternatively, you can right click on the file within the note review queue, and access the same options:

![note-review-queue-context-menu](https://github.com/user-attachments/assets/d4affa19-5126-45f8-bf3c-0079d2a8a597)

The note will then be scheduled appropriately by the [learning algorithm](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/algorithms/)
, and the markdown file updated:

![note-frontmatter](https://github.com/user-attachments/assets/b9744f50-c897-46ad-ab34-1bbc55796b57)

### Keyboard Shortcuts[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/notes/#keyboard-shortcuts "Permanent link")

The `Easy`, `Good`, and `Hard` review result can also be selected from the plugin's [command list](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/plugin-commands/)
.

This is less practical than the methods described above, but does enable the definition of keyboard shortcuts. You can create custom hotkeys for the review result in `Settings -> HotKeys`.

### Selecting a Note for Review[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/notes/#selecting-a-note-for-review "Permanent link")

There are a few ways to open a note for review:

*   Open a note via the standard Obsidian features
*   Double click on a note title from the Note Review Queue
*   Click on the `Spaced Repetition Status Area` in the status bar at the bottom of the screen
*   Select the command [Open a note to review review](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/plugin-commands/)
    

There are also the following relevant options:

*   [Open a random note for review](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/user-options/)
    
*   [Open next note automatically after a review](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/user-options/)
    

Multiple Note Review Decks[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/notes/#multiple-note-review-decks "Permanent link")

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

By default, there is a single review deck called `#review`.

This default tag can be changed in the [settings](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/user-options/#note-settings)
. Multiple review decks can also be specified.

Spaced Repetition Status Area[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/notes/#spaced-repetition-status-area "Permanent link")

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`Review: N note(s)` on the status bar at the bottom of the screen shows how many notes one has to review today (Today's notes + overdue notes).

Clicking on that opens one of the notes for review.

Back to top

---

# Contributing - Obsidian Spaced Repetition

 

[Skip to content](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/contributing/#contributing)

Contributing[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/contributing/#contributing "Permanent link")

==================================================================================================================

First off, thanks for wanting to contribute to the Spaced Repetition plugin!

Bug Reports & Feature Requests[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/contributing/#bug-reports-feature-requests "Permanent link")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Check the [roadmap](https://github.com/st3v3nmw/obsidian-spaced-repetition/projects/2/)
     for upcoming features & fixes.
*   Raise an issue [here](https://github.com/st3v3nmw/obsidian-spaced-repetition/issues/)
     if you have a feature request or a bug report.
*   Visit the [discussions](https://github.com/st3v3nmw/obsidian-spaced-repetition/discussions/)
     section for Q&A help, feedback, and general discussion.

Translating[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/contributing/#translating "Permanent link")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The plugin has been translated into the following languages by the Obsidian community 😄.

*   Arabic / العربية
*   Chinese (Simplified) / 简体中文
*   Chinese (Traditional) / 繁體中文
*   Czech / čeština
*   Dutch / Nederlands
*   French / français
*   German / Deutsch
*   Italian / Italiano
*   Korean / 한국어
*   Japanese / 日本語
*   Polish / Polski
*   Portuguese (Brazil) / Português do Brasil
*   Spanish / Español
*   Russian / русский
*   Turkish / Türkçe

### Steps[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/contributing/#steps "Permanent link")

To help translate the plugin to your language:

1.  Fork the [repository](https://github.com/st3v3nmw/obsidian-spaced-repetition)
    .
2.  Copy the entries from `src/lang/locale/en.ts` to the proper file in `src/lang/locale/` (i.e. `fr.ts` for French, or `sw.ts` for Swahili). The locale codes are [IETF language tags](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/IETF_language_tag)
    .
3.  Translate,
4.  Then open a pull request,

### Example[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/contributing/#example "Permanent link")

Sample `en.ts` file:

`[](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/contributing/#__codelineno-0-1) // English [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/contributing/#__codelineno-0-2) [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/contributing/#__codelineno-0-3) export default { [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/contributing/#__codelineno-0-4)     EASY: "Easy", [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/contributing/#__codelineno-0-5)     SHOW_ANSWER: "Show Answer", [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/contributing/#__codelineno-0-6)     DAYS_STR_IVL: "${interval} days", [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/contributing/#__codelineno-0-7)     CHECK_ALGORITHM_WIKI: [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/contributing/#__codelineno-0-8)         'For more information, check the <a href="${algoUrl}">algorithm implementation</a>.', [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/contributing/#__codelineno-0-9) };`

Equivalent `sw.ts` file:

`[](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/contributing/#__codelineno-1-1) // Swahili [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/contributing/#__codelineno-1-2) [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/contributing/#__codelineno-1-3) export default { [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/contributing/#__codelineno-1-4)     EASY: "Rahisi", [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/contributing/#__codelineno-1-5)     SHOW_ANSWER: "Onyesha Jibu", [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/contributing/#__codelineno-1-6)     DAYS_STR_IVL: "Siku ${interval}", [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/contributing/#__codelineno-1-7)     CHECK_ALGORITHM_WIKI: [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/contributing/#__codelineno-1-8)         'Kwa habari zaidi, angalia <a href="${algoUrl}">utekelezaji wa algorithm</a>.', [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/contributing/#__codelineno-1-9) };`

A part of that last one is uhh, Google translated, I have a working understanding of Swahili but not enough to write computerese lol.

Please note that:

1.  Only the strings(templates) on the right of the key should be translated.
2.  Text inside `${}` isn't translated. This is used to replace variables in code. For instance, if interval = 4, it becomes `4 days` in English & `Siku 4` in Swahili. Quite nifty if you ask me.

* * *

Code[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/contributing/#code "Permanent link")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### General changes[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/contributing/#general-changes "Permanent link")

1.  Make your changes.
2.  Run `pnpm dev` to watch for changes & rebuild the plugin automatically.
3.  You could create symbolic links between the build files and the Obsidian vault, example:
    
    `[](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/contributing/#__codelineno-2-1) # remove existing files in the Obsidian vault [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/contributing/#__codelineno-2-2) rm ~/notes/.obsidian/plugins/obsidian-spaced-repetition/main.js ~/notes/.obsidian/plugins/obsidian-spaced-repetition/manifest.json ~/notes/.obsidian/plugins/obsidian-spaced-repetition/styles.css [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/contributing/#__codelineno-2-3) # use absolute paths [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/contributing/#__codelineno-2-4) ln -s /home/stephen/obsidian-spaced-repetition/build/main.js /home/stephen/notes/.obsidian/plugins/obsidian-spaced-repetition [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/contributing/#__codelineno-2-5) ln -s /home/stephen/obsidian-spaced-repetition/manifest.json /home/stephen/notes/.obsidian/plugins/obsidian-spaced-repetition [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/contributing/#__codelineno-2-6) ln -s /home/stephen/obsidian-spaced-repetition/styles.css /home/stephen/notes/.obsidian/plugins/obsidian-spaced-repetition`
    
    *   This can be coupled with the [Hot Reload plugin](https://github.com/pjeby/hot-reload)
        
4.  Document the "user-facing" changes e.g. new feature, UI change, etc.
    
5.  If your "business logic" is properly decoupled from Obsidian APIs, write some unit tests.
    *   This project uses [jest](https://jestjs.io/)
        , tests are stored in `tests/`.
    *   `pnpm test`
6.  Before pushing your changes, run the linter: `pnpm lint`
    *   Format the code in case any warnings are raised: `pnpm format`
7.  Open the pull request.

### UI changes[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/contributing/#ui-changes "Permanent link")

*   All UI changes should be made in the `src/gui/` folder.
    
*   Put your changes under the right section (see "MARK:" or "#region" comments in the code).
    
*   Document your functions & classes with JSDoc.
    
*   One can switch between mobile view and desktop view by entering the following command in developer console:
    
    `[](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/contributing/#__codelineno-3-1) this.app.emulateMobile(false); // to switch to desktop view [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/contributing/#__codelineno-3-2) [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/contributing/#__codelineno-3-3) this.app.emulateMobile(true); // to switch to mobile view`
    
*   Test your changes in all arrangements that the ui can be in:
    
    1.  Desktop
    2.  Mobile portrait mode
    3.  Small sized mobile device
    4.  Mobile landscape mode
    5.  Tablet landscape mode
    6.  Tablet portrait mode
    7.  All the above, but with tab view option enabled
    8.  All the above, but with tab view option disabled
    9.  All the above, but with tab view option disabled and different flashcard height/width percentages

* * *

Documentation[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/contributing/#documentation "Permanent link")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The documentation consists of Markdown files which [MkDocs](https://www.mkdocs.org/)
 converts to static web pages. Specifically, this project uses [MkDocs Material](https://squidfunk.github.io/mkdocs-material/getting-started/)
.

These files reside in `docs/docs/` in the respective language's folder. For instance, English docs are located in `docs/docs/en/`.

The docs are served on [https://www.stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/](https://www.stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/)
.

For small changes, you can simply open an pull request for merging (against the `master` branch). The changes will be live once a new [release](https://github.com/st3v3nmw/obsidian-spaced-repetition/releases)
 is made.

For larger diffs, it's important that you check how your docs look like as explained below.

### Viewing Docs Locally[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/contributing/#viewing-docs-locally "Permanent link")

#### Initial Setup[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/contributing/#initial-setup "Permanent link")

1.  Create a virtual environment: `python3 -m venv venv`
2.  Activate it: `. venv/bin/activate`
3.  Install the required dependencies: `pip install -r requirements.txt`

#### Viewing[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/contributing/#viewing "Permanent link")

1.  Activate the virtual environment: `. venv/bin/activate`
2.  Serve the docs: `mkdocs serve`
3.  View your documentation locally on [http://127.0.0.1:8000/obsidian-spaced-repetition/](http://127.0.0.1:8000/obsidian-spaced-repetition/)
    , any changes you make will reflect on the browser instantly.

### Translating Documentation[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/contributing/#translating-documentation "Permanent link")

1.  Create a folder for your language in `docs/docs/` if it doesn't exist. Use the language codes provided [here](https://squidfunk.github.io/mkdocs-material/setup/changing-the-language/#site-language)
    .
2.  Add the code from (1) to the MkDocs configuration (`mkdocs.yml` - `plugins.i18n.languages`).
3.  Copy the files from the English (`en`) folder into the new folder.
4.  Translate then open a pull request.

* * *

Maintenance[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/contributing/#maintenance "Permanent link")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### Releases[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/contributing/#releases "Permanent link")

Example using `v1.9.2`:

1.  Create a new branch: `git switch -c release-v1.9.2`
2.  Bump the plugin version in `manifest.json` and `package.json` (following [Semantic Versioning](https://semver.org/spec/v2.0.0.html)
    ).
    *   Semantic Versioning TL;DR, given a version number `MAJOR.MINOR.PATCH`, increment the:
        *   `MAJOR` version when you make incompatible API changes
        *   `MINOR` version when you add functionality in a backwards compatible manner
        *   `PATCH` version when you make backwards compatible bug fixes
    *   If the new version uses new Obsidian APIs, update `minAppVersion` and `versions.json` to reflect this.
3.  Run `pnpm changelog` to update the CHANGELOG.
4.  Commit and push the changes:
    
    `[](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/contributing/#__codelineno-4-1) git add . [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/contributing/#__codelineno-4-2) git commit -m "chore: bump version to v1.9.2" [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/contributing/#__codelineno-4-3) git push --set-upstream origin release-v1.9.2`
    
5.  Open and merge the PR into `master`.
    
6.  Locally, switch back to `master` and pull the changes: `git switch master && git pull`
7.  Create a git tag with the version: `git tag -a 1.9.2 -m "1.9.2"`
8.  Push the tag: `git push --tags`.  
    You're all set! [This GitHub action](https://github.com/st3v3nmw/obsidian-spaced-repetition/blob/master/.github/workflows/release.yml)
     should pick it up, create a release, publish it, and update the live documentation.

Back to top

---

# Spaced Repetition Guides - Obsidian Spaced Repetition

 

[Skip to content](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/resources/#spaced-repetition-resources)

Spaced Repetition Resources[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/resources/#spaced-repetition-resources "Permanent link")

=============================================================================================================================================

General[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/resources/#general "Permanent link")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [How to Remember Anything Forever-Ish by Nicky Case](https://ncase.me/remember/)
    
*   [Spaced Repetition for Efficient Learning by Gwern](https://www.gwern.net/Spaced-repetition/)
    
*   [20 rules of knowledge formulation by Dr. Piotr Wozniak](https://supermemo.guru/wiki/20_rules_of_knowledge_formulation)
     is a great introduction on proper flashcard creation.

* * *

Flashcards[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/resources/#flashcards "Permanent link")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [PRODUCTIVELY Learning New Things Using Obsidian by @FromSergio](https://youtu.be/DwSNZEW6jCU)
    

* * *

Notes[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/resources/#notes "Permanent link")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Notes should be atomic i.e. focus on a single concept.
*   Notes should be highly linked.
*   Reviews should start only after properly understanding a concept.
*   Reviews should be [Feynman-technique](https://fs.blog/2021/02/feynman-learning-technique/)
    \-esque.

### Incremental Writing[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/resources/#incremental-writing "Permanent link")

*   English: [Obsidian: inbox review with spaced repetition by @aviskase](https://youtu.be/zG5r7QIY_TM)
    
*   Russian / русский: [Разгребатель инбокса заметок как у Andy Matuschak в Obsidian by @YuliyaBagriy\_ru](https://youtu.be/CF6SSHB74cs)
    

Improvement Needed

Extract anything important from the reference and include here instead

This was introduced [here](https://github.com/st3v3nmw/obsidian-spaced-repetition/issues/15)
 by `@aviskase`.

#### Brief summary[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/resources/#brief-summary "Permanent link")

Andy Matuschak uses [spaced repetition system for working on writing inbox](https://notes.andymatuschak.org/z7iCjRziX6V6unNWL81yc2dJicpRw2Cpp9MfQ)
.

Improvement Needed

What does this mean?

In short, there are four possible actions (where `x < y`):

*   skip note (increase interval for `x`) == mark as `good`
*   work on it, mark as fruitful work (decrease interval) == mark as `hard`
*   work on it, mark as unfruitful work (increase interval for `y`) == mark as `easy`
*   convert to evergreen note (stop using the space-repetition prompts)

Back to top

---

---

# Cards with Blank Lines - Obsidian Spaced Repetition

 

[Skip to content](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/cards-with-blank-lines/#including-blank-lines-in-flashcards)

Including Blank Lines in Flashcards[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/cards-with-blank-lines/#including-blank-lines-in-flashcards "Permanent link")

=====================================================================================================================================================================================

By default, [Multi-line Basic](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/q-and-a-cards/#multi-line-basic)
, [Multi-line Bidirectional](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/q-and-a-cards/#multi-line-bidirectional)
 and [Cloze](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/cloze-cards/)
 type flashcards recognize a blank line as the end of the flashcard text. This means that blank lines can not be included within the text.

If blank lines need to be included (e.g. on a card containing a markdown table), the `Characters denoting the end of clozes and multiline flashcards` [setting](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/user-options/#flashcard-separators)
 needs to be changed.

For example, it could be changed to `+++`.

Global Edit Required

Note that after changing this you have to manually edit any flashcards you already have.

Including a Table in the Flashcard Answer[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/cards-with-blank-lines/#including-a-table-in-the-flashcard-answer "Permanent link")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Obsidian requires a blank line before a table for it to be displayed correctly.

Without it, Obsidian displays it just as text and not correctly formatted.

![table-with-no-preceding-blank-line](https://github.com/user-attachments/assets/daed1309-3b38-4d14-bb42-b302efda96df)

And with a blank line after the `?` and before the table, it is displays correctly. ![table-with-preceding-blank-line](https://github.com/user-attachments/assets/beef90b7-324e-4876-b10b-055a4d23d41f)

However, by default a blank line signifies the end of the multiline card.

To include the blank line, the `Characters denoting the end of clozes and multiline flashcards` [setting](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/user-options/#flashcard-separators)
 needs to be changed. Then that character sequence added as a line after the end of the flashcard text. For example:

![table-with-preceding-blank-line+++](https://github.com/user-attachments/assets/954fd7fc-6d5f-4315-b40e-2192664c3962)

Now the card is displayed correctly during a review.

![table-with-preceding-blank-line-review](https://github.com/user-attachments/assets/3bff8d25-f91f-4bc0-b922-7471d6b60869)

Including Blank Lines in a Cloze Flashcard[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/cards-with-blank-lines/#including-blank-lines-in-a-cloze-flashcard "Permanent link")

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

With `Convert ==highlights== to clozes` enabled in [settings](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/user-options/#flashcard-separators)
 and the `Characters denoting the end of clozes and multiline flashcards` set to `+++`, we can have blank lines in a cloze flashcard. E.g.

![cloze-with-blank-lines](https://github.com/user-attachments/assets/f9d6f123-3378-41cb-9c93-2b061856c81d)

As there are 3 clozes defined, three separate cards will be generated for review. One card, for example is:

![cloze-with-blank-lines-front1](https://github.com/user-attachments/assets/6b939d46-b93a-4a67-96d4-6985ccafb76e)

And after `Show Answer` is clicked, the following is displayed:

![cloze-with-blank-lines-answer](https://github.com/user-attachments/assets/225abd90-20a4-4e29-abb3-36beb61388d7)

Limitation[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/cards-with-blank-lines/#limitation "Permanent link")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### Blank Lines in Answer Side Only[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/cards-with-blank-lines/#blank-lines-in-answer-side-only "Permanent link")

Blank lines are only supported in the answer side of a multiline flashcard, and not in the question side.

Back to top

---

# Cloze Cards - Obsidian Spaced Repetition

 

[Skip to content](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/cloze-cards/#cloze-cards)

Cloze Cards[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/cloze-cards/#cloze-cards "Permanent link")

==========================================================================================================================

With [Single & Multiline Cards](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/q-and-a-cards/)
 the text of both the front and back of each card is specified.

With `cloze` cards a single text is specified, together with an identification of which parts of the text should be obscured.

The front of the card is displayed as the text with (one or more) `cloze deletions` obscured.

Cloze Deletions[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/cloze-cards/#cloze-deletions "Permanent link")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

A part of the card text is identified as a cloze deletion by surrounding it with the `cloze delimiter`.

### Single Cloze Deletion[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/cloze-cards/#single-cloze-deletion "Permanent link")

By default, the cloze delimiter is `==`, and a simple cloze card would be:

`[](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/cloze-cards/#__codelineno-0-1) The first female prime minister of Australia was ==Julia Gillard==`

Displayed when reviewed

Initial View

The first female prime minister of Australia was \[...\]

After `Show Answer` Clicked

The first female prime minister of Australia was Julia Gillard

### Multiple Cloze Deletions[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/cloze-cards/#multiple-cloze-deletions "Permanent link")

If the card text identifies multiple parts as cloze deletions, then multiple cards will be shown for review, each one occluding one deletion, while leaving the other deletions visible.

For instance, the following note:

`[](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/cloze-cards/#__codelineno-1-1) The first female ==prime minister== of Australia was ==Julia Gillard==`

Card 1 Initial View

The first female \[...\] of Australia was Julia Gillard

Card 2 Initial View

The first female prime minister of Australia was \[...\]

After `Show Answer` Clicked (same for both cards)

The first female prime minister of Australia was Julia Gillard

These two cards are considered sibling cards. See [sibling cards](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/flashcards-overview/#sibling-cards)
 regarding the [Bury sibling cards until the next day](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/user-options/#flashcard-review)
 scheduling option.

Cloze Types[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/cloze-cards/#cloze-types "Permanent link")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### Simplified Clozes[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/cloze-cards/#simplified-clozes "Permanent link")

Simplified Clozes are the Cloze Type we have been using so far. They keep working as before, but now you can add hints to them. That means each card will occlude one deletion, showing its hint if available, while leaving the other deletions visible.

For instance, the following note:

`[](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/cloze-cards/#__codelineno-2-1) This ==note== doesn't need to have ==number==^[hint] on clozes`

Will generate two cards, with the following fronts:

1.  `This [...] doesn't need to have number on clozes`
2.  `This note doesn't need to have [hint] on clozes`

And both will have the same back:

`[](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/cloze-cards/#__codelineno-3-1) This note doesn't need to have number on clozes`

### Classic Clozes[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/cloze-cards/#classic-clozes "Permanent link")

Classic Clozes are the same as Simplified Clozes, but they also have a sequence number used to sort and group deletions.

For instance, the following note:

`[](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/cloze-cards/#__codelineno-4-1) This is a ==cloze==^[a hint][^1]. This is ==too, but without hint==[^2]. And this one is asked ==together with the first cloze==[^1].`

Will generate two cards, with the following fronts:

1.  `This is a [a hint]. This is too, but without hint. And this one is asked [...].`
2.  `This is a cloze. This [...]. And this one is asked together with the first cloze.`

And both will have the same back:

`[](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/cloze-cards/#__codelineno-5-1) This is a cloze. This is too, but without hint. And this one is asked together with the first cloze.`

### Generalized Cloze Overlapping[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/cloze-cards/#generalized-cloze-overlapping "Permanent link")

The Cloze Overlapping Generalization allows you to dictate the behavior of each deletion individually. Each deletion has its own set of actions that indicate how it will behave on each card:

*   `a` for ask (hide the deletion answer in the front of the card while showing it in the back).
*   `h` for hide (hide the deletion answer both in the front and back of the card).
*   `s` for show (show the deletion answer both in the front and back of the card).

For instance, the following note:

`[](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/cloze-cards/#__codelineno-6-1) ==Some context for items 2 and 4, but that could spoil items 1 and 3. Note that this doesn't even need to be asked==[^hshs] [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/cloze-cards/#__codelineno-6-2) . [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/cloze-cards/#__codelineno-6-3) - ==Item 1==[^ashh] [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/cloze-cards/#__codelineno-6-4) - ==Item 2==[^hash] [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/cloze-cards/#__codelineno-6-5) - ==Item 3==[^hhas] [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/cloze-cards/#__codelineno-6-6) - ==Item 4==[^hhha]`

In this example, 4 cards will be generated, where items 1 to 4 will be asked sequentially. When asking Item 1, all other text will be hidden. When asking Item 2, just the Item 1 and the context will be displayed. When asking Item 3, only the Item 2 will be displayed. Finally, when asking Item 4, both the Item 3 and the context text will be displayed.

Custom Cloze Patterns[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/cloze-cards/#custom-cloze-patterns "Permanent link")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can now create your own Cloze Patterns. For instance, to emulate Anki-like clozes (e.g., `{{1::text::hint}}`), simply add the following pattern to your settings:

`[](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/cloze-cards/#__codelineno-7-1) {{[123::]answer[::hint]}}`

Brackets `[]` delineate where the sequence number and hint will be placed, along with any additional characters of your choice (e.g., the `::` in the example above). Clozecraft automatically generates a regex pattern based on your custom pattern. Sequence numbers are identified by finding numbers between brackets, hints by finding the word `hint` in brackets, and the deleted text by finding the word `answer`.

Here are some examples of custom patterns:

| Explanation | Pattern in the Settings | Simplified Cloze Usage | Numbered Cloze Usage | Generalized Cloze Overlapping Usage |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Anki-Like Pattern | `{{[123::]answer[::hint]}}` | `Brazilians speak {{Portuguese}}`  <br>  <br>Or, with hint:  <br>`Brazilians speak {{Portuguese::language}}` | `Brazilians speak {{1::Portuguese}}`  <br>  <br>Or, with hint:  <br>`Brazilians speak {{1::Portuguese::language}}` | `Brazilians speak {{a::Portuguese}}`  <br>  <br>Or, with hint:  <br>`Brazilians speak {{a::Portuguese::language}}` |
| Highlighted pattern with hint and sequencer in footnotes. | `==answer==[^\\[hint\\]][\\[^123\\]]` | `Brazilians speak ==Portuguese==`  <br>  <br>Or, with hint:  <br>`Brazilians speak ==Portuguese==^[language]` | `Brazilians speak ==Portuguese==[^1]`  <br>  <br>Or, with hint:  <br>`Brazilians speak ==Portuguese==^[language][^1]` | `Brazilians speak ==Portuguese==[^a]`  <br>  <br>Or, with hint:  <br>`Brazilians speak ==Portuguese==^[language][^a]` |

Warning

Make sure that your custom cloze patterns do not conflict with other flashcard separators.  
For instance, the Anki-Like pattern `{{[123::]answer[::hint]}}` conflicts with the default single line flashcard separator `::`.

Warning

You can use brackets as part of your pattern, but you need to [escape](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Escape_character)
 them with `\\`.  
For instance, in the pattern `==answer==[^\\[hint\\]][\\[^123\\]]`, the brackets _inside_ the outer brackets are escaped (`^\\[hint\\]` & `\\[^123\\]`).

In your settings, you can add multiple patterns at once, separating them with a new line:

`[](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/cloze-cards/#__codelineno-8-1) {{[123::]answer[::hint]}} [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/cloze-cards/#__codelineno-8-2) ==answer==[^\\[hint\\]][\\[^123\\]]`

Then, you can use them in your notes:

`[](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/cloze-cards/#__codelineno-9-1) This note has both ==highlighted clozes==[^1] and {{2::anki like clozes}} [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/cloze-cards/#__codelineno-9-2) [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/cloze-cards/#__codelineno-9-3) And this note has both ==highlighted clozes==^[footnote hint][^1] and {{2::anki like clozes::anki like hint}}`

Warning

Remember, deletions must be of the same Cloze Type. You can't mix, for instance, a Classic Cloze with a Simplified Cloze in the same note, as they employ different ways to sort and identify the cards.

Back to top

---

# Organizing into Decks - Obsidian Spaced Repetition

 

[Skip to content](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/decks/#organizing-into-decks)

Organizing into Decks[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/decks/#organizing-into-decks "Permanent link")

========================================================================================================================================

![flashcard-decks-1](https://github.com/user-attachments/assets/a207b0f6-b064-443c-9c55-540681b10891)

Using Obsidian Tags[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/decks/#using-obsidian-tags "Permanent link")

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  Specify flashcard tags in settings (`#flashcards` is the default).
2.  Tag any notes that you'd like to put flashcards using said tags.

### Hierarchical Tags[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/decks/#hierarchical-tags "Permanent link")

Note that `#flashcards` will match nested tags like `#flashcards/subdeck/subdeck`.

### Multiple Tags Within a Single File[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/decks/#multiple-tags-within-a-single-file "Permanent link")

A single file can contain cards for multiple different decks.

This is possible because a tag pertains to all subsequent cards in a file until any subsequent tag.

For example:

`[](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/decks/#__codelineno-0-1) #flashcards/deckA [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/decks/#__codelineno-0-2) Question1 (in deckA)::Answer1 [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/decks/#__codelineno-0-3) Question2 (also in deckA)::Answer2 [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/decks/#__codelineno-0-4) Question3 (also in deckA)::Answer3 [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/decks/#__codelineno-0-5) [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/decks/#__codelineno-0-6) #flashcards/deckB [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/decks/#__codelineno-0-7) Question4 (in deckB)::Answer4 [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/decks/#__codelineno-0-8) Question5 (also in deckB)::Answer5 [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/decks/#__codelineno-0-9) [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/decks/#__codelineno-0-10) #flashcards/deckC [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/decks/#__codelineno-0-11) Question6 (in deckC)::Answer6`

### A Single Card Within Multiple Decks[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/decks/#a-single-card-within-multiple-decks "Permanent link")

Usually the content of a card is only relevant to a single deck. However, sometimes content doesn't fall neatly into a single deck of the hierarchy.

In these cases, a card can be tagged as being part of multiple decks. The following card is specified as being in the three different decks listed.

`[](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/decks/#__codelineno-1-1) #flashcards/language/words #flashcards/trivia #flashcards/learned-from-tv [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/decks/#__codelineno-1-2) A group of cats is called a::clowder`

Note that as shown in the above example, all tags must be placed on the same line, separated by spaces.

### Question Specific Tags[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/decks/#question-specific-tags "Permanent link")

A tag that is present at the start of the first line of a card is "question specific", and applies only to that card.

For example:

`[](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/decks/#__codelineno-2-1) #flashcards/deckA [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/decks/#__codelineno-2-2) Question1 (in deckA)::Answer1 [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/decks/#__codelineno-2-3) Question2 (also in deckA)::Answer2 [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/decks/#__codelineno-2-4) Question3 (also in deckA)::Answer3 [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/decks/#__codelineno-2-5) [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/decks/#__codelineno-2-6) #flashcards/deckB Question4 (in deckB)::Answer4 [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/decks/#__codelineno-2-7) [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/decks/#__codelineno-2-8) Question6 (in deckA)::Answer6`

Here `Question6` will be part of `deckA` and not `deckB` as `deckB` is specific to `Question4` only.

* * *

Using Folder Structure[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/decks/#using-folder-structure "Permanent link")

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The plugin will automatically search for folders that contain flashcards & use their paths to create decks & sub-decks

e.g. `Folder/sub-folder/sub-sub-folder` ⇔ `Deck/sub-deck/sub-sub-deck`.

This is an alternative to the tagging option and can be enabled in [settings](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/user-options/#tags-folders)
.

Back to top

---

# Flashcards Overview - Obsidian Spaced Repetition

 

[Skip to content](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/flashcards-overview/#flashcard-introduction)

Flashcard Introduction[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/flashcards-overview/#flashcard-introduction "Permanent link")

========================================================================================================================================================

Flashcards are defined within standard Obsidian markdown files.

A markdown file containing flashcards must identify the [deck](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/decks/)
 (or decks) into which the flashcards are placed. However, the file does not need to be tagged as a [note](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/notes/)
 for it to have flashcards defined.

Two types of flashcards are supported:

Question & Answer

[Question & Answer](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/q-and-a-cards/)
 flashcards are ones where the flashcard text contains both the question text and answer text.

* * *

![flashcard-qanda-example](https://github.com/user-attachments/assets/65639d80-b249-4b16-ae40-c2af011c6aab)

Cloze

[Cloze](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/cloze-cards/)
 flashcards are ones where the flashcard text identifies parts of the text (e.g. a word or phrase) that is hidden when the front of the card is shown.  
The hidden text is known as a `cloze deletion`.

* * *

![flashcard-cloze-example](https://github.com/user-attachments/assets/9fb12f2e-9b81-45d9-9097-7f1e3d97ae5a)

Tip

For guidelines on how to write and structure flashcards, see [Spaced Repetition Guides](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/resources/#flashcards)

* * *

Flashcard Text, Flashcards and Cards[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/flashcards-overview/#flashcard-text-flashcards-and-cards "Permanent link")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Note

For simplicity `flashcard text` is sometimes written just as `flashcard`

The `flashcard text` is text that defines the type and content of a card (or a set of related, `sibling` cards).

### Single flashcard, multiple cards[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/flashcards-overview/#single-flashcard-multiple-cards "Permanent link")

For some flashcard types, the flashcard text defines a single card. For other flashcard types, multiple cards are defined.

| Flashcard Type | Cards Defined |
| --- | --- |
| [Single-line Basic](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/q-and-a-cards/#single-line-basic) | flashcard defines the front and back of a single card. |
| [Single-line Bidirectional](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/q-and-a-cards/#single-line-bidirectional) | flashcard defines two cards. |
| [Multi-line Basic](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/q-and-a-cards/#multi-line-basic) | flashcard defines the front and back of a single card. |
| [Multi-line Bidirectional](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/q-and-a-cards/#multi-line-bidirectional) | flashcard defines two cards. |
| [Cloze](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/cloze-cards/) | flashcard defines multiple cards, the number of cards based on the number of cloze deletions. |

### Sibling Cards[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/flashcards-overview/#sibling-cards "Permanent link")

If there are multiple cards defined by a single flashcard, those cards are known as `sibling` cards.

A special scheduling option is available for the review of sibling cards. If the [Bury sibling cards until the next day](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/user-options/#flashcard-review)
 setting is turned on, only one sibling card is available for review on a single day.

### Including Blank Lines within Multiline and Cloze Flashcards[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/flashcards-overview/#including-blank-lines-within-multiline-and-cloze-flashcards "Permanent link")

By default, the end of a multiline flashcard is denoted by a blank line at the end of the flashcard text. This means that blank lines can not be included within the text.

See [Cards with Blank Lines](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/cards-with-blank-lines/)
 if blank lines need to be included.

* * *

RTL Support[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/flashcards-overview/#rtl-support "Permanent link")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

There are two ways that the plugin can be used with RTL languages, such as Arabic, Hebrew, Persian (Farsi).

If all cards are in a RTL language, then simply enable the global Obsidian option `Editor → Right-to-left (RTL)`.

If all cards within a single note have the same LTR/RTL direction, then frontmatter can be used to specify the text direction. For example:

`[](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/flashcards-overview/#__codelineno-0-1) --- [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/flashcards-overview/#__codelineno-0-2) direction: rtl [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/flashcards-overview/#__codelineno-0-3) ---`

This is the same way text direction is specified to the `RTL Support` plugin.

Note that there is no current support for cards with different text directions within the same note.

* * *

Card Maintenance[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/flashcards-overview/#card-maintenance "Permanent link")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### Deleting cards[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/flashcards-overview/#deleting-cards "Permanent link")

To delete a card, simply delete the scheduling information & the card text.

### Ignoring cards[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/flashcards-overview/#ignoring-cards "Permanent link")

You can wrap flashcards in HTML comments e.g. `<!--Card text <!--SR:2021-08-20,13,290--> -->` to prevent it from showing up in your review queues. You can always remove the wrapping comment later.

Back to top

---

# Question & Answer Cards - Obsidian Spaced Repetition

 

[Skip to content](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/q-and-a-cards/#question-answer-cards)

Question & Answer Cards[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/q-and-a-cards/#question-answer-cards "Permanent link")

==================================================================================================================================================

Note

Cards must be assigned to a deck, either using an Obsidian tag such as `#flashcard` or by using the folder structure within the vault.

See [Decks](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/decks/)
 for further details.

Single-line Basic[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/q-and-a-cards/#single-line-basic "Permanent link")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The prompt and the answer are separated by `::` (this can be configured in [settings](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/user-options/#flashcard-separators)
).

`[](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/q-and-a-cards/#__codelineno-0-1) the question goes on this side::answer goes here!`

Displayed when reviewed

Card Front

the question goes on this side

Card Back

answer goes here!

Single-line Bidirectional[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/q-and-a-cards/#single-line-bidirectional "Permanent link")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Two cards are created from the single flashcard text.

The two parts are separated by `:::` (this can be configured in [settings](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/user-options/#flashcard-separators)
).

For example:

`[](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/q-and-a-cards/#__codelineno-1-1) info 1:::info 2`

Card 1

Front

info 1

Back

info 2

Card 2

Front

info 2

Back

info 1

These two cards are considered sibling cards. See [sibling cards](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/flashcards-overview/#sibling-cards)
 regarding the [Bury sibling cards until the next day](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/user-options/#flashcard-review)
 scheduling option.

* * *

Multi-line Basic[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/q-and-a-cards/#multi-line-basic "Permanent link")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The front and the back of the card are separated by `?` (this can be configured in [settings](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/user-options/#flashcard-separators)
).

`[](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/q-and-a-cards/#__codelineno-2-1) As per the definition [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/q-and-a-cards/#__codelineno-2-2) of "multiline" the prompt [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/q-and-a-cards/#__codelineno-2-3) can be on multiple lines [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/q-and-a-cards/#__codelineno-2-4) ? [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/q-and-a-cards/#__codelineno-2-5) same goes for [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/q-and-a-cards/#__codelineno-2-6) the answer`

Displayed when reviewed

Card Front

As per the definition  
of "multiline" the prompt  
can be on multiple lines

Card Back

same goes for  
the answer

These can also span over multiple lines as long as both sides "touch" the `?`.

See [Cards with Blank Lines](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/cards-with-blank-lines/)
 if blank lines need to be included.

* * *

Multi-line Bidirectional[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/q-and-a-cards/#multi-line-bidirectional "Permanent link")

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Two cards are created from the single flashcard text.

The two parts are separated by `??` (this can be configured in [settings](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/user-options/#flashcard-separators)
).

For example:

`[](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/q-and-a-cards/#__codelineno-3-1) info 1A [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/q-and-a-cards/#__codelineno-3-2) info 1B [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/q-and-a-cards/#__codelineno-3-3) info 1C [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/q-and-a-cards/#__codelineno-3-4) ?? [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/q-and-a-cards/#__codelineno-3-5) info 2A [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/q-and-a-cards/#__codelineno-3-6) info 2B`

These can also span over multiple lines as long as both sides "touch" the `??`: To include blank lines, see the section below.

Card 1

Front

info 1A  
info 1B  
info 1C

Back

info 2A  
info 2B

Card 2

Front

info 2A  
info 2B

Back

info 1A  
info 1B  
info 1C

These two cards are considered sibling cards. See [sibling cards](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/flashcards-overview/#sibling-cards)
 regarding the [Bury sibling cards until the next day](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/user-options/#flashcard-review)
 scheduling option.

Back to top

---

# Reviewing & Cramming - Obsidian Spaced Repetition

 

[Skip to content](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/reviewing/#reviewing-cramming)

Reviewing & Cramming[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/reviewing/#reviewing-cramming "Permanent link")

========================================================================================================================================

A key part of spaced repetition learning is being shown the front of cards to test whether or not you recall the information on the back. There are two similar functions that perform this – [reviewing](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/reviewing/#reviewing)
 & [cramming](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/reviewing/#cramming)
.

Reviewing

For the selected deck, you are only shown  
new cards (i.e. ones that have never been reviewed before) as well as  
due cards (those that the [algorithm](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/algorithms/)
 has decided it's time to review)

Cramming

You are shown every single card in the selected deck/note, even those that have recently been reviewed.

Common Features of Reviewing & Cramming[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/reviewing/#common-features-of-reviewing-cramming "Permanent link")

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### Deck Selection[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/reviewing/#deck-selection "Permanent link")

Although you may want to review or cram all cards across all decks, you often may wish to do so on only a subset of decks.

![flashcard-decks-1](https://github.com/user-attachments/assets/a207b0f6-b064-443c-9c55-540681b10891)

All subdecks included

For example, clicking on the `course` deck will also include all cards within the `aws` and `developer-associate` decks.

### Operation[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/reviewing/#operation "Permanent link")

![review-operation](https://github.com/user-attachments/assets/d8f438dc-f1f0-43c4-a752-a5eeb64346e4)

!!! note "" # | Name | Description - | - | - 1 | Edit | Edit the flashcard text 2 | Reset | Reset the review schedule information - the review interval is set to 1 day, and the ease is set to the default value 3 | Info | Shows the scheduling information for the card 4 | Skip | Skip the current card without reviewing

### Context[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/reviewing/#context "Permanent link")

If the parent note has heading(s), the flashcard will have a title containing the context.

Taking the following note:

`[](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/reviewing/#__codelineno-0-1) #flashcards [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/reviewing/#__codelineno-0-2) [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/reviewing/#__codelineno-0-3) # Trivia [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/reviewing/#__codelineno-0-4) [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/reviewing/#__codelineno-0-5) ## Capitals [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/reviewing/#__codelineno-0-6) [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/reviewing/#__codelineno-0-7) ### Africa [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/reviewing/#__codelineno-0-8) [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/reviewing/#__codelineno-0-9) Kenya::Nairobi [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/reviewing/#__codelineno-0-10) [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/reviewing/#__codelineno-0-11) ### North America [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/reviewing/#__codelineno-0-12) [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/reviewing/#__codelineno-0-13) Canada::Ottawa`

Context displayed

![reviewing-context](https://github.com/user-attachments/assets/2ccfc23a-a106-4133-91ec-8bd0efd0e372)

Note

Context is only shown if enabled in [UI Preferences](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/user-options/#ui-preferences)

### Keyboard shortcuts[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/reviewing/#keyboard-shortcuts "Permanent link")

To review faster, use the following keyboard shortcuts:

*   `Space/Enter` => Show answer
*   `0` => Reset card's progress (Sorta like `Again` in Anki)
*   `1` => Review as `Hard`
*   `2` => Review as `Good`
*   `3` => Review as `Easy`

* * *

Reviewing[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/reviewing/#reviewing "Permanent link")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Once done creating cards, click on the flashcards button on the left ribbon to start reviewing the flashcards. After a card is reviewed, a HTML comment is added containing the next review day, the interval, and the card's ease.

`[](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/reviewing/#__codelineno-1-1) <!--SR:!2021-08-20,13,290-->`

Wrapping in a HTML comment makes the scheduling information not visible in the notes preview. For single-line cards, you can choose whether you want the HTML comment on the same line or on a separate line in the settings. Putting them on the same line prevents breaking of list structures in the preview or after auto-formatting.

Note that you can skip a card by simply pressing `S` (case doesn't matter).

Tip

If you're experiencing issues with the size of the modal on mobile devices, go to [settings](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/user-options/#ui-preferences)
 and set the _Flashcard Height Percentage_ and _Flashcard Width Percentage_ to 100% to maximize it.

* * *

Cramming[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/reviewing/#cramming "Permanent link")

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You are shown every single card, even those that have recently been reviewed. By using the appropriate [command](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/plugin-commands/)
 have the choice of cramming cards:

| Cards | Command |
| --- | --- |
| Within a single note | `Spaced Repetition: Cram flashcards in this note` |
| Within a deck (including all subdecks) | `Spaced Repetition: Select a deck to cram note` |

Back to top

---

# Statistics - Obsidian Spaced Repetition

 

[Skip to content](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/statistics/#statistics)

Statistics
==========

Statistics[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/statistics/#statistics "Permanent link")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The statistics section can be accessed in the `Statistics` section in the plugin's settings.

### Forecast[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/statistics/#forecast "Permanent link")

Stats on the number of cards due in the future.

![](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/st3v3nmw/obsidian-spaced-repetition/master/docs/media/en/stats_forecast.png)

### Intervals[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/statistics/#intervals "Permanent link")

Stats on delays until cards are shown again.

### Eases[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/statistics/#eases "Permanent link")

Stats on card eases.

### Card Types[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/statistics/#card-types "Permanent link")

Stats on card types: New, Young, Mature (Have intervals more than 1 month).

# Index - Obsidian Spaced Repetition

 

[跳转至](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/#obsidian-spaced-repetition)

Obsidian Spaced Repetition[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/#obsidian-spaced-repetition "Permanent link")

====================================================================================================================================

![](https://img.shields.io/github/downloads/st3v3nmw/obsidian-spaced-repetition/total) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/downloads/st3v3nmw/obsidian-spaced-repetition/latest/total?style=flat-square) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/manifest-json/v/st3v3nmw/obsidian-spaced-repetition?style=flat-square)

在 Obsidian 上，通过间隔重复法，复习闪卡和笔记，对抗遗忘曲线。

开始使用

查看[快速预览](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/#quick-demo)
  
[插件安装](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/#installation)
指南  
间断重复学习[通用指南与技巧](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/resources/)

核心功能

[记忆闪卡](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/flashcards-overview/)
     [笔记](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/notes/)
  
[个性化设置](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/user-options/)
     [快捷指令](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/plugin-commands/)

* * *

[重复算法](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/algorithms/)
     [数据存储](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/data-storage/)

帮助与支持

访问 [讨论区](https://github.com/st3v3nmw/obsidian-spaced-repetition/discussions/)
 获取问题解答、反馈建议和常规讨论  
如果您想请求新功能或报告bug，在[这里](https://github.com/st3v3nmw/obsidian-spaced-repetition/issues/)
提交议题

贡献

在Obsidian社区的帮助下,插件已支持[十余种语言](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/contributing/#translating)
😄。若要添加对您语言的支持，请点击[翻译指南](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/contributing/#translating)
  
软件开发者可参与 [功能优化和 bug 修复](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/contributing/#code)

* * *

快速预览[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/#_1 "Permanent link")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![用户界面总览](https://github.com/user-attachments/assets/977bab30-cc5e-4b5c-849e-3881d82b3f8e)

1.  展示[笔记复习队列](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/notes/#note-review-queue)
      
    
2.  笔记复习队列  
    
3.  呼出Obsidian命令面板以访问[快捷指令](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/plugin-commands/)
      
    
4.  `闪卡复习按钮`选择要[复习](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/reviewing/#reviewing)
    的[卡组](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/reviewing/#deck-selection)
      
    
5.  标识该笔记闪卡所属 `#flashcards/science/physics` [卡组](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/decks/#using-obsidian-tags)
      
    
6.  [单行基础卡组](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/q-and-a-cards/#single-line-basic)
     (通过`::`分隔问题和答案)  
    
7.  [HTML注释](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/data-storage/#individual-markdown-files)
    显示复习计划  
    
8.  `Spaced Repetition 状态栏` 显示待复习的笔记和闪卡数量。点击[打开待复习笔记](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/notes/#selecting-a-note-for-review)
    

* * *

安装[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/#_2 "Permanent link")

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

您可以在 Obsidian 的社区插件商店轻松安装本插件 (搜索 `Spaced Repetition`)。

### 手动安装[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/#_3 "Permanent link")

高级

在您仓库的`.obsidian/plugins`目录下创建`obsidian-spaced-repetition`文件夹。下载[最新发行版](https://github.com/st3v3nmw/obsidian-spaced-repetition/releases)
，并将`main.js`，`manifest.json`和`styles.css`文件添加到该文件夹下。

* * *

支持我[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/#_4 "Permanent link")

# Repetition Algorithms - Obsidian Spaced Repetition

 

[跳转至](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/algorithms/#_1)

学习算法[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/algorithms/#_1 "Permanent link")

=================================================================================================

学习算法使用公式决定何时复习一个笔记或记忆闪卡。

| 算法  | 开发情况 |
| --- | --- |
| [SM-2-OSR](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/algorithms/#sm-2-osr) | 已实现 |
| [FSRS](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/algorithms/#fsrs) | 计划中 |
| [用户自定义间隔](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/algorithms/#user-specified-intervals) | 计划中 |

SM-2-OSR[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/algorithms/#sm-2-osr "Permanent link")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   `SM-2-OSR` 是 [Anki](https://faqs.ankiweb.net/what-spaced-repetition-algorithm.html)
     所采用的基于 [SM-2 算法](https://www.supermemo.com/en/archives1990-2015/english/ol/sm2)
    的变种。
*   使用三档打分制（记得/简单/较难）
*   初始熟练度会根据关联笔记的平均熟练度、当前笔记的重要性和基础熟练度加权计算（使用 最大外链因子）
*   Anki 还会加入少量的随机“扰动”，以防止同时创建且评级相同的卡片复习周期相同，导致总在同一天被复习。
*   除 PageRanks 之外，笔记和卡片复习均采用相同算法。

### 算法细节[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/algorithms/#_2 "Permanent link")

警告

该条目长时间未更新, 请注意参见 [源代码](https://github.com/st3v3nmw/obsidian-spaced-repetition/blob/master/src/algorithms/osr/srs-algorithm-osr.ts)

*   当存在外链时: 初始熟练度 = (1 - 链接加权) \_ 基础熟练度 + 链接加权 \_ 外链平均熟练度
*   链接加权 = 最大外链因子 \* min(1.0, log(外链数目 + 0.5) / log(64)) (以自适应不同情况)
    *   不同概念/笔记的优先级由 PageRank 算法设定（笔记之间存在轻重缓急）
        *   大多数情况下基础概念/笔记具有更高优先级
*   当用户对某个概念/笔记的自评为：
    *   简单, 熟练度增加 20 复习间隔更新为 原复习间隔 \_ 更新后熟练度 / 100 \_ 1.3 (1.3 是简单奖励)
    *   记得, 熟练度不变，复习间隔更新为 原复习间隔 \* old\_ease / 100
    *   困难, 熟练度降低 20，复习间隔更新为 原复习间隔 \* 0.5
        *   0.5 可在设置中更改
        *   最小熟练度 = 130
    *   当复习间隔不小于 8 天时
        *   间隔 += 随机取值({-扰动, 0, +扰动})
            *   设定 扰动 = 向上取整(0.05 \* 间隔)
            *   Anki 文档: > "\[...\] Anki 还会加入少量的随机扰动，以防止同时出现且评级相同的卡片获得相同的复习周期，导致其它们是在同一天被复习。"
*   复习计划信息将被存储于笔记的YAML front matter。

* * *

FSRS[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/algorithms/#fsrs "Permanent link")

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

算法详情参见：[fsrs4anki](https://github.com/open-spaced-repetition/fsrs4anki/wiki)

本插件目前尚未集成该算法，进展参见： [\[FEAT\] sm-2 is outdated, can you please replace it with the fsrs algorithm? #748](https://github.com/st3v3nmw/obsidian-spaced-repetition/issues/748)

* * *

用户自定义间隔[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/algorithms/#_3 "Permanent link")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

这可能是最简单的“算法”了：允许用户为复习结果设置固定间隔天数。

例如：`较难` --> 1天

本插件目前尚未集成该算法，进展参见： [\[FEAT\] user defined "Easy, Good, Hard" values instead of or in addition to the algorithm defined one. #741](https://github.com/st3v3nmw/obsidian-spaced-repetition/issues/741)

回到页面顶部
