# Contributing - Obsidian Spaced Repetition

 

[跳转至](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/contributing/#_1)

贡献[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/contributing/#_1 "Permanent link")

=================================================================================================

首先，感谢您想为 Spaced Repetition 插件做出贡献！

报告Bug & 功能请求[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/contributing/#bug "Permanent link")

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   查看 [路线图](https://github.com/st3v3nmw/obsidian-spaced-repetition/projects/2/)
     以了解即将推出的功能和修复。
*   如果您想请求新功能或报告Bug，请点击[这里](https://github.com/st3v3nmw/obsidian-spaced-repetition/issues/)
    。
*   前往[讨论区](https://github.com/st3v3nmw/obsidian-spaced-repetition/discussions/)
    参与问答互助、意见反馈和常规讨论。

翻译[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/contributing/#_2 "Permanent link")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

在 Obsidian 社区的帮助下，插件已支持如下语言。😄

*   Arabic / العربية
*   Chinese (Simplified) / 简体中文
*   Chinese (Traditional) / 繁體中文
*   Czech / čeština
*   French / français
*   German / Deutsch
*   Italian / Italiano
*   Korean / 한국어
*   Japanese / 日本語
*   Polish / Polski
*   Portuguese (Brazil) / Português do Brasil
*   Spanish / Español
*   Russian / русский
*   Turkish / Türkçe

### 步骤[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/contributing/#_3 "Permanent link")

若要添加对您语言的支持，请按如下步骤操作：

1.  Fork [代码仓库](https://github.com/st3v3nmw/obsidian-spaced-repetition)
    。
2.  将 `src/lang/locale/en.ts` 中的内容复制到 `src/lang/locale/` 目录下对应的文件 (例如：`fr.ts` 对应法语, `sw.ts` 对应斯瓦希里语)。 本地化代码应符合 [IETF 语言标签规范](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/IETF_language_tag)
    。
3.  进行翻译。
4.  提交Pull Request。

### 示例[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/contributing/#_4 "Permanent link")

样例`en.ts`文件:

`[](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/contributing/#__codelineno-0-1) // English [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/contributing/#__codelineno-0-2) [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/contributing/#__codelineno-0-3) export default { [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/contributing/#__codelineno-0-4)     EASY: "Easy", [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/contributing/#__codelineno-0-5)     SHOW_ANSWER: "Show Answer", [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/contributing/#__codelineno-0-6)     DAYS_STR_IVL: "${interval} days", [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/contributing/#__codelineno-0-7)     CHECK_ALGORITHM_WIKI: [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/contributing/#__codelineno-0-8)         'For more information, check the <a href="${algoUrl}">algorithm implementation</a>.', [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/contributing/#__codelineno-0-9) };`

对应的`sw.ts`文件:

`[](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/contributing/#__codelineno-1-1) // Swahili [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/contributing/#__codelineno-1-2) [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/contributing/#__codelineno-1-3) export default { [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/contributing/#__codelineno-1-4)     EASY: "Rahisi", [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/contributing/#__codelineno-1-5)     SHOW_ANSWER: "Onyesha Jibu", [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/contributing/#__codelineno-1-6)     DAYS_STR_IVL: "Siku ${interval}", [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/contributing/#__codelineno-1-7)     CHECK_ALGORITHM_WIKI: [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/contributing/#__codelineno-1-8)         'Kwa habari zaidi, angalia <a href="${algoUrl}">utekelezaji wa algorithm</a>.', [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/contributing/#__codelineno-1-9) };`

最后一部分,呃...其实用了谷歌翻译。虽然我对斯瓦希里语有实际理解，但还不足以写计算机术语哈哈。

请注意:

1.  只需翻译键名右侧的字符串（模板）。
2.  不要翻译 `${}` 里的内容。这个占位符用于代码变量替换。例如：如果 interval = 4，英语会显示`4 days`，斯瓦希里语则会是`Siku 4`。是不是很巧妙？

* * *

代码[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/contributing/#_5 "Permanent link")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 常规更改[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/contributing/#_6 "Permanent link")

1.  修改代码。
2.  运行`pnpm dev`来查看变化和自动重构插件。
3.  您可以在 构建文件 和 Obsidian vault 间创建符号链接，如：
    
    `[](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/contributing/#__codelineno-2-1) # 从 Obsidian vault 移除现有插件文件 [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/contributing/#__codelineno-2-2) rm ~/notes/.obsidian/plugins/obsidian-spaced-repetition/main.js ~/notes/.obsidian/plugins/obsidian-spaced-repetition/manifest.json ~/notes/.obsidian/plugins/obsidian-spaced-repetition/styles.css [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/contributing/#__codelineno-2-3) # 使用绝对路径 [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/contributing/#__codelineno-2-4) ln -s /home/stephen/obsidian-spaced-repetition/build/main.js /home/stephen/notes/.obsidian/plugins/obsidian-spaced-repetition [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/contributing/#__codelineno-2-5) ln -s /home/stephen/obsidian-spaced-repetition/manifest.json /home/stephen/notes/.obsidian/plugins/obsidian-spaced-repetition [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/contributing/#__codelineno-2-6) ln -s /home/stephen/obsidian-spaced-repetition/styles.css /home/stephen/notes/.obsidian/plugins/obsidian-spaced-repetition`
    
    *   此过程可搭配 [Hot Reload 插件](https://github.com/pjeby/hot-reload)
        。
4.  请记录“面向用户”的修改，如：新增功能，UI调整，等等。
    
5.  如果您的“业务逻辑”与 Obsidian APIs 充分解耦，请写一些单元测试。
    *   本项目使用 [jest](https://jestjs.io/)
        , 测试文件存放在`tests/`目录。
    *   `pnpm test`
6.  在推送您的修改前，请执行 linter：`pnpm lint`
    *   如果出现任何警告，请格式化代码: `pnpm format`
7.  提交 Pull Request。

### UI 修改[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/contributing/#ui "Permanent link")

*   所有 UI 修改都应当在`src/gui/`目录内完成。
    
*   将修改放在正确的区域 (参考代码中的 "MARK:" 或 "#region" 注释)。
    
*   用 JSDoc 为你的函数和类编写文档。
    
*   您可以在开发者控制台中输入以下代码来切换桌面端和移动端视图。
    
    `[](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/contributing/#__codelineno-3-1) this.app.emulateMobile(false); // 切换至桌面端视图 [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/contributing/#__codelineno-3-2) [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/contributing/#__codelineno-3-3) this.app.emulateMobile(true); // 切换至移动端视图`
    
*   在以下所有布局中测试您的 UI 修改:
    
    1.  桌面端
    2.  移动端竖屏模式
    3.  小尺寸移动设备
    4.  移动端横屏模式
    5.  平板横屏模式
    6.  平板竖屏模式
    7.  上述所有场景 + 启用标签视图
    8.  上述所有场景 + 禁用标签视图
    9.  上述所有场景 + 禁用标签视图 + 卡片不同长宽比

* * *

文档[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/contributing/#_7 "Permanent link")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

文档由 Markdown 文件构成，并通过[MkDocs](https://www.mkdocs.org/)
 转换为静态网页。 特别地，本项目采用 [MkDocs Material](https://squidfunk.github.io/mkdocs-material/getting-started/)
。

这些文件存放于`docs/docs/`相应的语言文件夹内。例如，英文文档位于 `docs/docs/en/`目录下。

文档托管于[https://www.stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/](https://www.stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/)
。

对于微小改动，您可以仅提交 Pull Request 来合并(针对 `master` 分支)。 这些修改将在新[发行版](https://github.com/st3v3nmw/obsidian-spaced-repetition/releases)
发布时生效。

对于大幅改动，您必须如下所述，检查文档外观。

### 本地查看文档[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/contributing/#_8 "Permanent link")

#### 初始化[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/contributing/#_9 "Permanent link")

1.  创建虚拟环境：`python3 -m venv venv`
2.  激活虚拟环境：`. venv/bin/activate`
3.  安装项目依赖：`pip install -r requirements.txt`

#### 查看[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/contributing/#_10 "Permanent link")

1.  激活虚拟环境: `. venv/bin/activate`
2.  部署文档网页: `mkdocs serve`
3.  打开[http://127.0.0.1:8000/obsidian-spaced-repetition/](http://127.0.0.1:8000/obsidian-spaced-repetition/)
    以在本地查看文档，您的任何修改都会立即在浏览器上反映。

### 翻译文档[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/contributing/#_11 "Permanent link")

1.  如果您的语言未出现在 `docs/docs/` 中，请为您的语言创建一个新文件夹。使用[这里](https://squidfunk.github.io/mkdocs-material/setup/changing-the-language/#site-language)
    提供的语言代码为文件夹命名。
2.  将 (1) 中的语言代码添加到 MkDocs 配置中(`mkdocs.yml` - `plugins.i18n.languages`)。
3.  将 `en` 目录下的英文文档复制到新文件夹中。
4.  翻译，再提交 Pull Request 。

* * *

维护[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/contributing/#_12 "Permanent link")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 发行版[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/contributing/#_13 "Permanent link")

以 `v1.9.2` 为例:

1.  创建一个新分支: `git switch -c release-v1.9.2`
2.  在 `manifest.json` 和 `package.json` 中更新版本号(遵循[Semantic Versioning](https://semver.org/spec/v2.0.0.html)
    )。
    *   Semantic Versioning 速览：版本号格式为 `MAJOR.MINOR.PATCH`，增加:
        *   `MAJOR`（主版本号），当进行不兼容的 API 更改
        *   `MINOR`（次版本号），当添加向后兼容的新功能
        *   `PATCH`（修订版本号），当进行向后兼容的 bug 修复
    *   如果新版本使用新的 Obsidian APIs，请更新`minAppVersion`和`versions.json`以反映这一点。
3.  运行 `pnpm changelog` 以更新 CHANGELOG。
4.  提交并推送您的修改:
    
    `[](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/contributing/#__codelineno-4-1) git add . [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/contributing/#__codelineno-4-2) git commit -m "chore: bump version to v1.9.2" [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/contributing/#__codelineno-4-3) git push --set-upstream origin release-v1.9.2`
    
5.  提交合并到 `master` 分支的 Pull Request。
    
6.  在本地，切换到 `master` 分支并拉取修改： `git switch master && git pull`
7.  以版本号创建 git 标签： `git tag -a 1.9.2 -m "1.9.2"`
8.  推送标签: `git push --tags`.  
    您已经完成了所有流程！ [这个 GitHub action](https://github.com/st3v3nmw/obsidian-spaced-repetition/blob/master/.github/workflows/release.yml)
     会自动触发，创建一个发行版并发布，同时更新在线文档。

回到页面顶部

---

# Data Storage - Obsidian Spaced Repetition

 

[跳转至](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/data-storage/#_1)

数据存储[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/data-storage/#_1 "Permanent link")

===================================================================================================

复习计划信息[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/data-storage/#_2 "Permanent link")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 独立Markdown文件[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/data-storage/#markdown "Permanent link")

这是存储卡片和笔记的 复习计划信息 的默认方法。

对于卡片，信息存储在对应的 HTML 注释中。例如，对于卡片：

`[](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/data-storage/#__codelineno-0-1) The RCU and WCU limits for a single partition key value::3000 RCU, 1000 WCU`

复习后，会自动添加HTML注释：

`[](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/data-storage/#__codelineno-1-1) <!--SR:!2024-08-16,51,230-->`

默认情况下，注释会生成在卡片文本的下一行。  
您可以启用 [将计划重复时间保存在最后一行的同一行？](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/user-options/#storage-of-scheduling-data)
以在文本的同行生成注释。

笔记的复习计划信息存储在文件开头的 YAML frontmatter 中，例如：

![note-frontmatter](https://github.com/user-attachments/assets/b9744f50-c897-46ad-ab34-1bbc55796b57)

纯文本格式

* * *

sr-due: 2024-07-01 sr-interval: 3 sr-ease: 269

* * *

### 集中计划文件[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/data-storage/#_3 "Permanent link")

所有卡片和笔记的 复习计划信息 存储在统一专用文件中。

本插件目前尚未集成该方法，进展参见：

[\[FEAT\] Stop using YAML; Move plugin info and data to separate file #162](https://github.com/st3v3nmw/obsidian-spaced-repetition/issues/162)

* * *

个性化设置[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/data-storage/#_4 "Permanent link")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

所有用户 [设置选项](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/user-options/)
 存储在插件目录的 `data.json` 文件中。

* * *

卡片暂存列表[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/data-storage/#_5 "Permanent link")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

当某张卡片当天被复习过后，其 关联卡片 直至次日才会出现。

仅当 [将关联卡片隐藏至下一天？](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/user-options/#flashcard-review)
 选项启用时生效。

该信息同样存储在 `data.json` 文件。

注意

为节省存储空间，卡片完整内容将不被存储，仅保留简短的数字哈希值（"fingerprint"）

回到页面顶部

---

# Notes - Obsidian Spaced Repetition

 

[跳转至](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/notes/#_1)

笔记[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/notes/#_1 "Permanent link")

==========================================================================================

提示

关于如何编写和组织笔记的指南，请参见 [Spaced Repetition Guides](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/resources/#notes)

开始使用[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/notes/#_2 "Permanent link")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

为需复习的 Markdown 笔记添加 `note review` 标签（默认值是`#review`）

该笔记会出现在右侧边栏 `笔记复习序列` 的 `#review` 标签下。

注意

添加 `#review` 标签的笔记不会立即出现在笔记复习序列中。  
您需要点击 `复习卡片按钮` 或 `Spaced Repitition 状态栏` 以更新队列。

笔记复习序列[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/notes/#_3 "Permanent link")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![笔记复习序列](https://github.com/user-attachments/assets/c0e1d09c-610f-4775-b532-ab78369b117a)

注意

1.  笔记复习序列  
    
2.  `#review`标签下的卡组预览  
    
3.  新笔记，即新增`#review`标签但尚未复习的笔记  
    
4.  计划于 8 月 1 日复习的笔记  
    
5.  计划于 8 月 31 日复习的笔记  
    

### 显示笔记复习序列[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/notes/#_4 "Permanent link")

默认情况下，插件启动时会自动显示笔记复习序列（可在[设置](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/user-options/#note-settings)
中修改 `启动时开启复习笔记窗格`）

您也可以运行 `Open Notes Review Queue in sidebar` [快捷指令](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/plugin-commands/)
 以显示复习序列。

复习[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/notes/#_5 "Permanent link")

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

打开笔记，阅读并复习。完成后，根据您对笔记的理解程度，在菜单（三点图标）中选择 “复习：简单”，“复习：记得” 或 “复习：较难”。

![三点菜单](https://github.com/user-attachments/assets/5f37ab88-30f9-477d-b39c-eb86ba15abdb)

也可在 笔记复习序列 中右键笔记调出相同选项。

![笔记复习序列](https://github.com/user-attachments/assets/d4affa19-5126-45f8-bf3c-0079d2a8a597)

随后，笔记会根据 [学习算法](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/algorithms/)
 自动安排复习计划，并更新状态:

![笔记头部标签](https://github.com/user-attachments/assets/b9744f50-c897-46ad-ab34-1bbc55796b57)

### 快捷键[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/notes/#_6 "Permanent link")

您可以通过 [快捷指令](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/plugin-commands/)
 选择 `记得`，`简单`和`较难`。

虽然这不如上述方法便捷，但您可在`设置 -> 快捷键`中为其自定义快捷键。

### 选择笔记以复习[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/notes/#_7 "Permanent link")

您可以通过如下方式选择笔记以复习:

*   使用 Obsidian 标准功能打开笔记
*   在 笔记复习序列 中双击笔记
*   点击窗口右下角的 `Spaced Repetition 状态栏`
*   快捷指令 [打开一个笔记开始复习](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/plugin-commands/)
    

相关选项还包括:

*   [随机打开一个笔记复习](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/user-options/)
    
*   [复习后自动打开下一个笔记](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/user-options/)
    

多个复习卡组[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/notes/#_8 "Permanent link")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

默认使用标签为 `#review` 的唯一卡组。

您可在 [设置](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/user-options/#note-settings)
 中修改默认标签，并添加更多复习卡组。

Spaced Repetition 状态栏[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/notes/#spaced-repetition "Permanent link")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

窗口右下角状态栏的 `复习：N 笔记` 显示今日需复习的笔记数量(今日笔记+逾期笔记)。

点击 状态栏 可打开一个笔记开始复习。

回到页面顶部

---

# Spaced Repetition Guides - Obsidian Spaced Repetition

 

[跳转至](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/resources/#_1)

相关资源[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/resources/#_1 "Permanent link")

================================================================================================

整体[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/resources/#_2 "Permanent link")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [《如何永远记忆任何知识》 by Nicky Case](https://ncase.me/remember/)
    
*   [《高效学习的重复间隔原理》 by Gwern](https://www.gwern.net/Spaced-repetition/)
    
*   [《20 条知识法则》 by Dr. Piotr Wozniak](https://supermemo.guru/wiki/20_rules_of_knowledge_formulation)
     是闪卡制作极佳指南。

* * *

记忆闪卡[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/resources/#_3 "Permanent link")

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [《使用Obsidian高效学习新知识》 by @FromSergio](https://youtu.be/DwSNZEW6jCU)
    

* * *

笔记[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/resources/#_4 "Permanent link")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   笔记应原子化。例如，专注于单一主题。
*   笔记之间应当高度关联。
*   先充分理解概念，再复习。
*   复习应采用[费曼学习法](https://fs.blog/2021/02/feynman-learning-technique/)
    。

### 渐进式写作[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/resources/#_5 "Permanent link")

*   英文: [PRODUCTIVELY Learning New Things Using Obsidian by @FromSergio](https://youtu.be/zG5r7QIY_TM)
    
*   俄文 / русский: [Разгребатель инбокса заметок как у Andy Matuschak в Obsidian by @YuliyaBagriy\_ru](https://youtu.be/CF6SSHB74cs)
    

待完善

从参考材料中提取要点，并放在此处。

点击[这里](https://github.com/st3v3nmw/obsidian-spaced-repetition/issues/15)
查看`@aviskase`的介绍。

#### 概要[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/resources/#_6 "Permanent link")

Andy Matuschak 使用[间隔重复系统处理写作素材库](https://notes.andymatuschak.org/z7iCjRziX6V6unNWL81yc2dJicpRw2Cpp9MfQ)
。

待完善

这说明什么？

简要来说，有四种可能的操作(其中 `x < y`):

*   跳过笔记 (增加 `x` 天的复习间隔) == 标记为 `记得`
*   已阅，认为有效 (降低复习间隔) == 标记为 `较难`
*   已阅，认为无效 (增加 `y` 天的复习间隔) == 标记为 `简单`
*   转换为长期笔记 (终止间隔重复提示)

回到页面顶部

---

# Cards with Blank Lines - Obsidian Spaced Repetition

 

[跳转至](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/cards-with-blank-lines/#including-blank-lines-in-flashcards)

Including Blank Lines in Flashcards[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/cards-with-blank-lines/#including-blank-lines-in-flashcards "Permanent link")

========================================================================================================================================================================================

By default, [Multi-line Basic](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/q-and-a-cards/#multi-line-basic)
, [Multi-line Bidirectional](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/q-and-a-cards/#multi-line-bidirectional)
 and [Cloze](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/cloze-cards/)
 type flashcards recognize a blank line as the end of the flashcard text. This means that blank lines can not be included within the text.

If blank lines need to be included (e.g. on a card containing a markdown table), the `Characters denoting the end of clozes and multiline flashcards` [setting](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/user-options/#flashcard-separators)
 needs to be changed.

For example, it could be changed to `+++`.

Global Edit Required

Note that after changing this you have to manually edit any flashcards you already have.

Including a Table in the Flashcard Answer[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/cards-with-blank-lines/#including-a-table-in-the-flashcard-answer "Permanent link")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Obsidian requires a blank line before a table for it to be displayed correctly.

Without it, Obsidian displays it just as text and not correctly formatted.

![table-with-no-preceding-blank-line](https://github.com/user-attachments/assets/daed1309-3b38-4d14-bb42-b302efda96df)

And with a blank line after the `?` and before the table, it is displays correctly. ![table-with-preceding-blank-line](https://github.com/user-attachments/assets/beef90b7-324e-4876-b10b-055a4d23d41f)

However, by default a blank line signifies the end of the multiline card.

To include the blank line, the `Characters denoting the end of clozes and multiline flashcards` [setting](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/user-options/#flashcard-separators)
 needs to be changed. Then that character sequence added as a line after the end of the flashcard text. For example:

![table-with-preceding-blank-line+++](https://github.com/user-attachments/assets/954fd7fc-6d5f-4315-b40e-2192664c3962)

Now the card is displayed correctly during a review.

![table-with-preceding-blank-line-review](https://github.com/user-attachments/assets/3bff8d25-f91f-4bc0-b922-7471d6b60869)

Including Blank Lines in a Cloze Flashcard[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/cards-with-blank-lines/#including-blank-lines-in-a-cloze-flashcard "Permanent link")

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

With `Convert ==highlights== to clozes` enabled in [settings](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/user-options/#flashcard-separators)
 and the `Characters denoting the end of clozes and multiline flashcards` set to `+++`, we can have blank lines in a cloze flashcard. E.g.

![cloze-with-blank-lines](https://github.com/user-attachments/assets/f9d6f123-3378-41cb-9c93-2b061856c81d)

As there are 3 clozes defined, three separate cards will be generated for review. One card, for example is:

![cloze-with-blank-lines-front1](https://github.com/user-attachments/assets/6b939d46-b93a-4a67-96d4-6985ccafb76e)

And after `Show Answer` is clicked, the following is displayed:

![cloze-with-blank-lines-answer](https://github.com/user-attachments/assets/225abd90-20a4-4e29-abb3-36beb61388d7)

Limitation[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/cards-with-blank-lines/#limitation "Permanent link")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### Blank Lines in Answer Side Only[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/cards-with-blank-lines/#blank-lines-in-answer-side-only "Permanent link")

Blank lines are only supported in the answer side of a multiline flashcard, and not in the question side.

回到页面顶部

---

# Organizing into Decks - Obsidian Spaced Repetition

 

[跳转至](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/decks/#organizing-into-decks)

Organizing into Decks[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/decks/#organizing-into-decks "Permanent link")

===========================================================================================================================================

![flashcard-decks-1](https://github.com/user-attachments/assets/a207b0f6-b064-443c-9c55-540681b10891)

Using Obsidian Tags[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/decks/#using-obsidian-tags "Permanent link")

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  Specify flashcard tags in settings (`#flashcards` is the default).
2.  Tag any notes that you'd like to put flashcards using said tags.

### Hierarchical Tags[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/decks/#hierarchical-tags "Permanent link")

Note that `#flashcards` will match nested tags like `#flashcards/subdeck/subdeck`.

### Multiple Tags Within a Single File[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/decks/#multiple-tags-within-a-single-file "Permanent link")

A single file can contain cards for multiple different decks.

This is possible because a tag pertains to all subsequent cards in a file until any subsequent tag.

For example:

`[](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/decks/#__codelineno-0-1) #flashcards/deckA [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/decks/#__codelineno-0-2) Question1 (in deckA)::Answer1 [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/decks/#__codelineno-0-3) Question2 (also in deckA)::Answer2 [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/decks/#__codelineno-0-4) Question3 (also in deckA)::Answer3 [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/decks/#__codelineno-0-5) [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/decks/#__codelineno-0-6) #flashcards/deckB [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/decks/#__codelineno-0-7) Question4 (in deckB)::Answer4 [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/decks/#__codelineno-0-8) Question5 (also in deckB)::Answer5 [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/decks/#__codelineno-0-9) [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/decks/#__codelineno-0-10) #flashcards/deckC [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/decks/#__codelineno-0-11) Question6 (in deckC)::Answer6`

### A Single Card Within Multiple Decks[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/decks/#a-single-card-within-multiple-decks "Permanent link")

Usually the content of a card is only relevant to a single deck. However, sometimes content doesn't fall neatly into a single deck of the hierarchy.

In these cases, a card can be tagged as being part of multiple decks. The following card is specified as being in the three different decks listed.

`[](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/decks/#__codelineno-1-1) #flashcards/language/words #flashcards/trivia #flashcards/learned-from-tv [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/decks/#__codelineno-1-2) A group of cats is called a::clowder`

Note that as shown in the above example, all tags must be placed on the same line, separated by spaces.

### Question Specific Tags[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/decks/#question-specific-tags "Permanent link")

A tag that is present at the start of the first line of a card is "question specific", and applies only to that card.

For example:

`[](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/decks/#__codelineno-2-1) #flashcards/deckA [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/decks/#__codelineno-2-2) Question1 (in deckA)::Answer1 [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/decks/#__codelineno-2-3) Question2 (also in deckA)::Answer2 [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/decks/#__codelineno-2-4) Question3 (also in deckA)::Answer3 [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/decks/#__codelineno-2-5) [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/decks/#__codelineno-2-6) #flashcards/deckB Question4 (in deckB)::Answer4 [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/decks/#__codelineno-2-7) [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/decks/#__codelineno-2-8) Question6 (in deckA)::Answer6`

Here `Question6` will be part of `deckA` and not `deckB` as `deckB` is specific to `Question4` only.

* * *

Using Folder Structure[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/decks/#using-folder-structure "Permanent link")

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The plugin will automatically search for folders that contain flashcards & use their paths to create decks & sub-decks

e.g. `Folder/sub-folder/sub-sub-folder` ⇔ `Deck/sub-deck/sub-sub-deck`.

This is an alternative to the tagging option and can be enabled in [settings](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/user-options/#tags-folders)
.

回到页面顶部

---

# Cloze Cards - Obsidian Spaced Repetition

 

[跳转至](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/cloze-cards/#cloze-cards)

Cloze Cards[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/cloze-cards/#cloze-cards "Permanent link")

=============================================================================================================================

With [Single & Multiline Cards](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/q-and-a-cards/)
 the text of both the front and back of each card is specified.

With `cloze` cards a single text is specified, together with an identification of which parts of the text should be obscured.

The front of the card is displayed as the text with (one or more) `cloze deletions` obscured.

Cloze Deletions[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/cloze-cards/#cloze-deletions "Permanent link")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

A part of the card text is identified as a cloze deletion by surrounding it with the `cloze delimiter`.

### Single Cloze Deletion[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/cloze-cards/#single-cloze-deletion "Permanent link")

By default, the cloze delimiter is `==`, and a simple cloze card would be:

`[](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/cloze-cards/#__codelineno-0-1) The first female prime minister of Australia was ==Julia Gillard==`

Displayed when reviewed

Initial View

The first female prime minister of Australia was \[...\]

After `Show Answer` Clicked

The first female prime minister of Australia was Julia Gillard

### Multiple Cloze Deletions[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/cloze-cards/#multiple-cloze-deletions "Permanent link")

If the card text identifies multiple parts as cloze deletions, then multiple cards will be shown for review, each one occluding one deletion, while leaving the other deletions visible.

For instance, the following note:

`[](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/cloze-cards/#__codelineno-1-1) The first female ==prime minister== of Australia was ==Julia Gillard==`

Card 1 Initial View

The first female \[...\] of Australia was Julia Gillard

Card 2 Initial View

The first female prime minister of Australia was \[...\]

After `Show Answer` Clicked (same for both cards)

The first female prime minister of Australia was Julia Gillard

These two cards are considered sibling cards. See [sibling cards](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/flashcards-overview/#sibling-cards)
 regarding the [Bury sibling cards until the next day](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/user-options/#flashcard-review)
 scheduling option.

Cloze Types[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/cloze-cards/#cloze-types "Permanent link")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### Simplified Clozes[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/cloze-cards/#simplified-clozes "Permanent link")

Simplified Clozes are the Cloze Type we have been using so far. They keep working as before, but now you can add hints to them. That means each card will occlude one deletion, showing its hint if available, while leaving the other deletions visible.

For instance, the following note:

`[](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/cloze-cards/#__codelineno-2-1) This ==note== doesn't need to have ==number==^[hint] on clozes`

Will generate two cards, with the following fronts:

1.  `This [...] doesn't need to have number on clozes`
2.  `This note doesn't need to have [hint] on clozes`

And both will have the same back:

`[](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/cloze-cards/#__codelineno-3-1) This note doesn't need to have number on clozes`

### Classic Clozes[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/cloze-cards/#classic-clozes "Permanent link")

Classic Clozes are the same as Simplified Clozes, but they also have a sequence number used to sort and group deletions.

For instance, the following note:

`[](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/cloze-cards/#__codelineno-4-1) This is a ==cloze==^[a hint][^1]. This is ==too, but without hint==[^2]. And this one is asked ==together with the first cloze==[^1].`

Will generate two cards, with the following fronts:

1.  `This is a [a hint]. This is too, but without hint. And this one is asked [...].`
2.  `This is a cloze. This [...]. And this one is asked together with the first cloze.`

And both will have the same back:

`[](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/cloze-cards/#__codelineno-5-1) This is a cloze. This is too, but without hint. And this one is asked together with the first cloze.`

### Generalized Cloze Overlapping[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/cloze-cards/#generalized-cloze-overlapping "Permanent link")

The Cloze Overlapping Generalization allows you to dictate the behavior of each deletion individually. Each deletion has its own set of actions that indicate how it will behave on each card:

*   `a` for ask (hide the deletion answer in the front of the card while showing it in the back).
*   `h` for hide (hide the deletion answer both in the front and back of the card).
*   `s` for show (show the deletion answer both in the front and back of the card).

For instance, the following note:

`[](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/cloze-cards/#__codelineno-6-1) ==Some context for items 2 and 4, but that could spoil items 1 and 3. Note that this doesn't even need to be asked==[^hshs] [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/cloze-cards/#__codelineno-6-2) . [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/cloze-cards/#__codelineno-6-3) - ==Item 1==[^ashh] [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/cloze-cards/#__codelineno-6-4) - ==Item 2==[^hash] [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/cloze-cards/#__codelineno-6-5) - ==Item 3==[^hhas] [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/cloze-cards/#__codelineno-6-6) - ==Item 4==[^hhha]`

In this example, 4 cards will be generated, where items 1 to 4 will be asked sequentially. When asking Item 1, all other text will be hidden. When asking Item 2, just the Item 1 and the context will be displayed. When asking Item 3, only the Item 2 will be displayed. Finally, when asking Item 4, both the Item 3 and the context text will be displayed.

Custom Cloze Patterns[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/cloze-cards/#custom-cloze-patterns "Permanent link")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can now create your own Cloze Patterns. For instance, to emulate Anki-like clozes (e.g., `{{1::text::hint}}`), simply add the following pattern to your settings:

`[](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/cloze-cards/#__codelineno-7-1) {{[123::]answer[::hint]}}`

Brackets `[]` delineate where the sequence number and hint will be placed, along with any additional characters of your choice (e.g., the `::` in the example above). Clozecraft automatically generates a regex pattern based on your custom pattern. Sequence numbers are identified by finding numbers between brackets, hints by finding the word `hint` in brackets, and the deleted text by finding the word `answer`.

Here are some examples of custom patterns:

| Explanation | Pattern in the Settings | Simplified Cloze Usage | Numbered Cloze Usage | Generalized Cloze Overlapping Usage |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Anki-Like Pattern | `{{[123::]answer[::hint]}}` | `Brazilians speak {{Portuguese}}`  <br>  <br>Or, with hint:  <br>`Brazilians speak {{Portuguese::language}}` | `Brazilians speak {{1::Portuguese}}`  <br>  <br>Or, with hint:  <br>`Brazilians speak {{1::Portuguese::language}}` | `Brazilians speak {{a::Portuguese}}`  <br>  <br>Or, with hint:  <br>`Brazilians speak {{a::Portuguese::language}}` |
| Highlighted pattern with hint and sequencer in footnotes. | `==answer==[^\\[hint\\]][\\[^123\\]]` | `Brazilians speak ==Portuguese==`  <br>  <br>Or, with hint:  <br>`Brazilians speak ==Portuguese==^[language]` | `Brazilians speak ==Portuguese==[^1]`  <br>  <br>Or, with hint:  <br>`Brazilians speak ==Portuguese==^[language][^1]` | `Brazilians speak ==Portuguese==[^a]`  <br>  <br>Or, with hint:  <br>`Brazilians speak ==Portuguese==^[language][^a]` |

Warning

Make sure that your custom cloze patterns do not conflict with other flashcard separators.  
For instance, the Anki-Like pattern `{{[123::]answer[::hint]}}` conflicts with the default single line flashcard separator `::`.

Warning

You can use brackets as part of your pattern, but you need to [escape](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Escape_character)
 them with `\\`.  
For instance, in the pattern `==answer==[^\\[hint\\]][\\[^123\\]]`, the brackets _inside_ the outer brackets are escaped (`^\\[hint\\]` & `\\[^123\\]`).

In your settings, you can add multiple patterns at once, separating them with a new line:

`[](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/cloze-cards/#__codelineno-8-1) {{[123::]answer[::hint]}} [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/cloze-cards/#__codelineno-8-2) ==answer==[^\\[hint\\]][\\[^123\\]]`

Then, you can use them in your notes:

`[](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/cloze-cards/#__codelineno-9-1) This note has both ==highlighted clozes==[^1] and {{2::anki like clozes}} [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/cloze-cards/#__codelineno-9-2) [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/cloze-cards/#__codelineno-9-3) And this note has both ==highlighted clozes==^[footnote hint][^1] and {{2::anki like clozes::anki like hint}}`

Warning

Remember, deletions must be of the same Cloze Type. You can't mix, for instance, a Classic Cloze with a Simplified Cloze in the same note, as they employ different ways to sort and identify the cards.

回到页面顶部

---

# Question & Answer Cards - Obsidian Spaced Repetition

 

[跳转至](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/q-and-a-cards/#question-answer-cards)

Question & Answer Cards[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/q-and-a-cards/#question-answer-cards "Permanent link")

=====================================================================================================================================================

Note

Cards must be assigned to a deck, either using an Obsidian tag such as `#flashcard` or by using the folder structure within the vault.

See [Decks](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/decks/)
 for further details.

Single-line Basic[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/q-and-a-cards/#single-line-basic "Permanent link")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The prompt and the answer are separated by `::` (this can be configured in [settings](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/user-options/#flashcard-separators)
).

`[](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/q-and-a-cards/#__codelineno-0-1) the question goes on this side::answer goes here!`

Displayed when reviewed

Card Front

the question goes on this side

Card Back

answer goes here!

Single-line Bidirectional[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/q-and-a-cards/#single-line-bidirectional "Permanent link")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Two cards are created from the single flashcard text.

The two parts are separated by `:::` (this can be configured in [settings](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/user-options/#flashcard-separators)
).

For example:

`[](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/q-and-a-cards/#__codelineno-1-1) info 1:::info 2`

Card 1

Front

info 1

Back

info 2

Card 2

Front

info 2

Back

info 1

These two cards are considered sibling cards. See [sibling cards](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/flashcards-overview/#sibling-cards)
 regarding the [Bury sibling cards until the next day](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/user-options/#flashcard-review)
 scheduling option.

* * *

Multi-line Basic[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/q-and-a-cards/#multi-line-basic "Permanent link")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The front and the back of the card are separated by `?` (this can be configured in [settings](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/user-options/#flashcard-separators)
).

`[](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/q-and-a-cards/#__codelineno-2-1) As per the definition [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/q-and-a-cards/#__codelineno-2-2) of "multiline" the prompt [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/q-and-a-cards/#__codelineno-2-3) can be on multiple lines [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/q-and-a-cards/#__codelineno-2-4) ? [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/q-and-a-cards/#__codelineno-2-5) same goes for [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/q-and-a-cards/#__codelineno-2-6) the answer`

Displayed when reviewed

Card Front

As per the definition  
of "multiline" the prompt  
can be on multiple lines

Card Back

same goes for  
the answer

These can also span over multiple lines as long as both sides "touch" the `?`.

See [Cards with Blank Lines](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/cards-with-blank-lines/)
 if blank lines need to be included.

* * *

Multi-line Bidirectional[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/q-and-a-cards/#multi-line-bidirectional "Permanent link")

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Two cards are created from the single flashcard text.

The two parts are separated by `??` (this can be configured in [settings](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/user-options/#flashcard-separators)
).

For example:

`[](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/q-and-a-cards/#__codelineno-3-1) info 1A [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/q-and-a-cards/#__codelineno-3-2) info 1B [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/q-and-a-cards/#__codelineno-3-3) info 1C [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/q-and-a-cards/#__codelineno-3-4) ?? [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/q-and-a-cards/#__codelineno-3-5) info 2A [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/q-and-a-cards/#__codelineno-3-6) info 2B`

These can also span over multiple lines as long as both sides "touch" the `??`: To include blank lines, see the section below.

Card 1

Front

info 1A  
info 1B  
info 1C

Back

info 2A  
info 2B

Card 2

Front

info 2A  
info 2B

Back

info 1A  
info 1B  
info 1C

These two cards are considered sibling cards. See [sibling cards](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/flashcards-overview/#sibling-cards)
 regarding the [Bury sibling cards until the next day](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/user-options/#flashcard-review)
 scheduling option.

回到页面顶部

---

# Flashcards Overview - Obsidian Spaced Repetition

 

[跳转至](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/flashcards-overview/#flashcard-introduction)

Flashcard Introduction[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/flashcards-overview/#flashcard-introduction "Permanent link")

===========================================================================================================================================================

Flashcards are defined within standard Obsidian markdown files.

A markdown file containing flashcards must identify the [deck](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/decks/)
 (or decks) into which the flashcards are placed. However, the file does not need to be tagged as a [note](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/notes/)
 for it to have flashcards defined.

Two types of flashcards are supported:

Question & Answer

[Question & Answer](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/q-and-a-cards/)
 flashcards are ones where the flashcard text contains both the question text and answer text.

* * *

![flashcard-qanda-example](https://github.com/user-attachments/assets/65639d80-b249-4b16-ae40-c2af011c6aab)

Cloze

[Cloze](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/cloze-cards/)
 flashcards are ones where the flashcard text identifies parts of the text (e.g. a word or phrase) that is hidden when the front of the card is shown.  
The hidden text is known as a `cloze deletion`.

* * *

![flashcard-cloze-example](https://github.com/user-attachments/assets/9fb12f2e-9b81-45d9-9097-7f1e3d97ae5a)

Tip

For guidelines on how to write and structure flashcards, see [Spaced Repetition Guides](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/resources/#flashcards)

* * *

Flashcard Text, Flashcards and Cards[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/flashcards-overview/#flashcard-text-flashcards-and-cards "Permanent link")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Note

For simplicity `flashcard text` is sometimes written just as `flashcard`

The `flashcard text` is text that defines the type and content of a card (or a set of related, `sibling` cards).

### Single flashcard, multiple cards[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/flashcards-overview/#single-flashcard-multiple-cards "Permanent link")

For some flashcard types, the flashcard text defines a single card. For other flashcard types, multiple cards are defined.

| Flashcard Type | Cards Defined |
| --- | --- |
| [Single-line Basic](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/q-and-a-cards/#single-line-basic) | flashcard defines the front and back of a single card. |
| [Single-line Bidirectional](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/q-and-a-cards/#single-line-bidirectional) | flashcard defines two cards. |
| [Multi-line Basic](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/q-and-a-cards/#multi-line-basic) | flashcard defines the front and back of a single card. |
| [Multi-line Bidirectional](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/q-and-a-cards/#multi-line-bidirectional) | flashcard defines two cards. |
| [Cloze](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/cloze-cards/) | flashcard defines multiple cards, the number of cards based on the number of cloze deletions. |

### Sibling Cards[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/flashcards-overview/#sibling-cards "Permanent link")

If there are multiple cards defined by a single flashcard, those cards are known as `sibling` cards.

A special scheduling option is available for the review of sibling cards. If the [Bury sibling cards until the next day](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/user-options/#flashcard-review)
 setting is turned on, only one sibling card is available for review on a single day.

### Including Blank Lines within Multiline and Cloze Flashcards[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/flashcards-overview/#including-blank-lines-within-multiline-and-cloze-flashcards "Permanent link")

By default, the end of a multiline flashcard is denoted by a blank line at the end of the flashcard text. This means that blank lines can not be included within the text.

See [Cards with Blank Lines](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/cards-with-blank-lines/)
 if blank lines need to be included.

* * *

RTL Support[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/flashcards-overview/#rtl-support "Permanent link")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

There are two ways that the plugin can be used with RTL languages, such as Arabic, Hebrew, Persian (Farsi).

If all cards are in a RTL language, then simply enable the global Obsidian option `Editor → Right-to-left (RTL)`.

If all cards within a single note have the same LTR/RTL direction, then frontmatter can be used to specify the text direction. For example:

`[](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/flashcards-overview/#__codelineno-0-1) --- [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/flashcards-overview/#__codelineno-0-2) direction: rtl [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/flashcards-overview/#__codelineno-0-3) ---`

This is the same way text direction is specified to the `RTL Support` plugin.

Note that there is no current support for cards with different text directions within the same note.

* * *

Card Maintenance[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/flashcards-overview/#card-maintenance "Permanent link")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### Deleting cards[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/flashcards-overview/#deleting-cards "Permanent link")

To delete a card, simply delete the scheduling information & the card text.

### Ignoring cards[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/flashcards-overview/#ignoring-cards "Permanent link")

You can wrap flashcards in HTML comments e.g. `<!--Card text <!--SR:2021-08-20,13,290--> -->` to prevent it from showing up in your review queues. You can always remove the wrapping comment later.

回到页面顶部

---

# Reviewing & Cramming - Obsidian Spaced Repetition

 

[跳转至](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/reviewing/#reviewing-cramming)

Reviewing & Cramming[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/reviewing/#reviewing-cramming "Permanent link")

===========================================================================================================================================

A key part of spaced repetition learning is being shown the front of cards to test whether or not you recall the information on the back. There are two similar functions that perform this – [reviewing](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/reviewing/#reviewing)
 & [cramming](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/reviewing/#cramming)
.

Reviewing

For the selected deck, you are only shown  
new cards (i.e. ones that have never been reviewed before) as well as  
due cards (those that the [algorithm](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/algorithms/)
 has decided it's time to review)

Cramming

You are shown every single card in the selected deck/note, even those that have recently been reviewed.

Common Features of Reviewing & Cramming[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/reviewing/#common-features-of-reviewing-cramming "Permanent link")

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### Deck Selection[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/reviewing/#deck-selection "Permanent link")

Although you may want to review or cram all cards across all decks, you often may wish to do so on only a subset of decks.

![flashcard-decks-1](https://github.com/user-attachments/assets/a207b0f6-b064-443c-9c55-540681b10891)

All subdecks included

For example, clicking on the `course` deck will also include all cards within the `aws` and `developer-associate` decks.

### Operation[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/reviewing/#operation "Permanent link")

![review-operation](https://github.com/user-attachments/assets/d8f438dc-f1f0-43c4-a752-a5eeb64346e4)

!!! note "" # | Name | Description - | - | - 1 | Edit | Edit the flashcard text 2 | Reset | Reset the review schedule information - the review interval is set to 1 day, and the ease is set to the default value 3 | Info | Shows the scheduling information for the card 4 | Skip | Skip the current card without reviewing

### Context[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/reviewing/#context "Permanent link")

If the parent note has heading(s), the flashcard will have a title containing the context.

Taking the following note:

`[](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/reviewing/#__codelineno-0-1) #flashcards [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/reviewing/#__codelineno-0-2) [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/reviewing/#__codelineno-0-3) # Trivia [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/reviewing/#__codelineno-0-4) [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/reviewing/#__codelineno-0-5) ## Capitals [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/reviewing/#__codelineno-0-6) [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/reviewing/#__codelineno-0-7) ### Africa [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/reviewing/#__codelineno-0-8) [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/reviewing/#__codelineno-0-9) Kenya::Nairobi [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/reviewing/#__codelineno-0-10) [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/reviewing/#__codelineno-0-11) ### North America [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/reviewing/#__codelineno-0-12) [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/reviewing/#__codelineno-0-13) Canada::Ottawa`

Context displayed

![reviewing-context](https://github.com/user-attachments/assets/2ccfc23a-a106-4133-91ec-8bd0efd0e372)

Note

Context is only shown if enabled in [UI Preferences](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/user-options/#ui-preferences)

### Keyboard shortcuts[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/reviewing/#keyboard-shortcuts "Permanent link")

To review faster, use the following keyboard shortcuts:

*   `Space/Enter` => Show answer
*   `0` => Reset card's progress (Sorta like `Again` in Anki)
*   `1` => Review as `Hard`
*   `2` => Review as `Good`
*   `3` => Review as `Easy`

* * *

Reviewing[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/reviewing/#reviewing "Permanent link")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Once done creating cards, click on the flashcards button on the left ribbon to start reviewing the flashcards. After a card is reviewed, a HTML comment is added containing the next review day, the interval, and the card's ease.

`[](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/reviewing/#__codelineno-1-1) <!--SR:!2021-08-20,13,290-->`

Wrapping in a HTML comment makes the scheduling information not visible in the notes preview. For single-line cards, you can choose whether you want the HTML comment on the same line or on a separate line in the settings. Putting them on the same line prevents breaking of list structures in the preview or after auto-formatting.

Note that you can skip a card by simply pressing `S` (case doesn't matter).

Tip

If you're experiencing issues with the size of the modal on mobile devices, go to [settings](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/user-options/#ui-preferences)
 and set the _Flashcard Height Percentage_ and _Flashcard Width Percentage_ to 100% to maximize it.

* * *

Cramming[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/reviewing/#cramming "Permanent link")

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You are shown every single card, even those that have recently been reviewed. By using the appropriate [command](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/plugin-commands/)
 have the choice of cramming cards:

| Cards | Command |
| --- | --- |
| Within a single note | `Spaced Repetition: Cram flashcards in this note` |
| Within a deck (including all subdecks) | `Spaced Repetition: Select a deck to cram note` |

回到页面顶部

---

# Statistics - Obsidian Spaced Repetition

 

[跳转至](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/statistics/#statistics)

Statistics
==========

Statistics[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/statistics/#statistics "Permanent link")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The statistics section can be accessed in the `Statistics` section in the plugin's settings.

### Forecast[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/statistics/#forecast "Permanent link")

Stats on the number of cards due in the future.

![](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/st3v3nmw/obsidian-spaced-repetition/master/docs/media/en/stats_forecast.png)

### Intervals[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/statistics/#intervals "Permanent link")

Stats on delays until cards are shown again.

### Eases[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/statistics/#eases "Permanent link")

Stats on card eases.

### Card Types[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/statistics/#card-types "Permanent link")

Stats on card types: New, Young, Mature (Have intervals more than 1 month).

# 卡片 - Obsidian Spaced Repetition

 

[跳转至](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/#_1)

卡片[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/#_1 "Permanent link")

===============================================================================================

新建卡片[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/#_2 "Permanent link")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[Piotr Wozniak的知识标准化二十守则](https://supermemo.guru/wiki/20_rules_of_knowledge_formulation)
 是创建复习卡片时的良好入门指南。

### 单行基础卡片 (Remnote风格)[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/#remnote "Permanent link")

问题和答案以 `::` 分隔（可在设置中更改）。

`[](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/#__codelineno-0-1) 这是问题::这是答案`

### 单行双向卡片[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/#_3 "Permanent link")

创建 `正:::反` 与其反向卡片 `反:::正`.

问题和答案以 `:::` 分隔（可在设置中更改）。

`[](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/#__codelineno-1-1) 这是问题:::这是答案`

注意：初次复习时插件会同时展示正向和反向卡片。 如果打开 **将关联卡片隐藏至下一天？** 将仅展示正向卡片。

### 多行基础卡片[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/#_4 "Permanent link")

卡片的正反面以 `?` 分隔（可在设置中更改）。

`[](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/#__codelineno-2-1) 多行卡片的正面 [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/#__codelineno-2-2) ? [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/#__codelineno-2-3) 多行卡片的反面`

只要正反面字段都在 `?` 的作用域内，卡片内容可以跨越多行:

`[](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/#__codelineno-3-1) 顾名思义 [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/#__codelineno-3-2) 多行卡片的内容 [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/#__codelineno-3-3) 可以跨越多行 [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/#__codelineno-3-4) ? [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/#__codelineno-3-5) 这也包括 [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/#__codelineno-3-6) 卡片的反面`

### 多行双向卡片[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/#_5 "Permanent link")

创建 `正??反` 与其反向卡片 `反??正`.

卡片的正反面以 `??` 分隔（可在设置中更改）。

`[](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/#__codelineno-4-1) 多行卡片的正面 [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/#__codelineno-4-2) ?? [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/#__codelineno-4-3) 多行卡片的反面`

只要正反面字段都在 `??` 的作用域内，卡片内容可以跨越多行:

`[](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/#__codelineno-5-1) 顾名思义 [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/#__codelineno-5-2) 多行卡片的内容 [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/#__codelineno-5-3) 可以跨越多行 [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/#__codelineno-5-4) ?? [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/#__codelineno-5-5) 这也包括 [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/#__codelineno-5-6) 卡片的反面`

注意：其隐藏机制同单行双向卡片

### 填空卡片[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/#_6 "Permanent link")

你可以轻松使用 `==高亮==` ，`**加粗**` ，或 `{{花括号}}` 创建挖空卡片.

该特性可在设置中开关。

暂不支持 Anki 风格的 `{{c1:This text}} would {{c2:generate}} {{c1:2 cards}}` 挖空语法。该特性正在 [计划中](https://github.com/st3v3nmw/obsidian-spaced-repetition/issues/93/)
。

卡组[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/#_7 "Permanent link")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![Screenshot from 2021-06-05 19-28-24](https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/43380836/120922211-78603400-c6d0-11eb-9d09-bdd5df1c9112.png)

卡组名称右边的绿色和蓝色数字分别表示到期卡片和新卡片数目。

### 使用 Obsidian 标签[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/#obsidian "Permanent link")

1.  在设置中设定制卡标签 (默认为 `#flashcards`)。
2.  将您想要制卡的笔记打上该标签。

#### 标签层级[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/#_8 "Permanent link")

注意 `#flashcards` 可以匹配嵌套标签例如 `#flashcards/subdeck/subdeck`.

#### 单个文件包含多个标签[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/#_9 "Permanent link")

单一文件中可以包含不同卡组的多个卡片内容。

这是因为一个标签的作用域直到下一个标签出现才会结束。

例如：

`[](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/#__codelineno-6-1) #flashcards/deckA [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/#__codelineno-6-2) Question1 (in deckA)::Answer1 [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/#__codelineno-6-3) Question2 (also in deckA)::Answer2 [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/#__codelineno-6-4) Question3 (also in deckA)::Answer3 [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/#__codelineno-6-5) [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/#__codelineno-6-6) #flashcards/deckB [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/#__codelineno-6-7) Question4 (in deckB)::Answer4 [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/#__codelineno-6-8) Question5 (also in deckB)::Answer5 [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/#__codelineno-6-9) [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/#__codelineno-6-10) #flashcards/deckC [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/#__codelineno-6-11) Question6 (in deckC)::Answer6`

#### 多个卡组包含同一卡片[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/#_10 "Permanent link")

通常情况下一张卡片只会出现在一个卡组。然而某些时候，一张卡片无法被恰当地归入单一卡组的层级结构中。

这种情况下，卡片可以被标记为归属为多个卡组。比如下面这张卡片属于三个卡组。

`[](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/#__codelineno-7-1) #flashcards/language/words #flashcards/trivia #flashcards/learned-from-tv [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/#__codelineno-7-2) A group of cats is called a::clowder`

注意，在上面的例子中所有标签必须位于一行并以空格隔开。

#### 作用于特定问答的卡片[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/#_11 "Permanent link")

位于卡片内容同一行开头处的标签是「仅限当前问答」的。

例如：

`[](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/#__codelineno-8-1) #flashcards/deckA [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/#__codelineno-8-2) Question1 (in deckA)::Answer1 [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/#__codelineno-8-3) Question2 (also in deckA)::Answer2 [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/#__codelineno-8-4) Question3 (also in deckA)::Answer3 [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/#__codelineno-8-5) [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/#__codelineno-8-6) #flashcards/deckB Question4 (in deckB)::Answer4 [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/#__codelineno-8-7) [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/#__codelineno-8-8) Question6 (in deckA)::Answer6`

此处 `Question6` 将出现在 `deckA` 但不会出现于 `deckB` 因 `deckB` 是仅作用于 `Question4` 的标签。

### 使用目录结构[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/#_12 "Permanent link")

插件将自动遍历目录结构并依次创建卡组和子卡组，例如 `Folder/sub-folder/sub-sub-folder` ⇔ `Deck/sub-deck/sub-sub-deck`。

这是使用标签指定卡组的替代方案，可以在设置中打开。

复习[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/#_13 "Permanent link")

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

注意您可以按 `S` 跳过一张卡片（大小写不敏感）。

提示

如果您在移动设备上遇到了悬浮框尺寸的问题，进入设置并将 _Flashcard Height Percentage_ 和 _Flashcard Width Percentage_ 设为 100% 以适应屏幕。

### 快速复习[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/#_14 "Permanent link")

你可以在快速复习中使用如下快捷键：

*   `Space/Enter` => 显示答案
*   `0` => 重置进度 (等价于 Anki 中的 `Again`)
*   `1` => 标记为 `Hard`
*   `2` 或 `Space` => 标记为 `Good`
*   `3` => 标记为 `Easy`

### 上下文[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/#_15 "Permanent link")

如用于制卡的部分位于笔记标题之下，则卡片中会附加一个上下文标题。

例如：

`[](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/#__codelineno-9-1) #flashcards [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/#__codelineno-9-2) [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/#__codelineno-9-3) # Trivia [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/#__codelineno-9-4) [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/#__codelineno-9-5) ## Capitals [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/#__codelineno-9-6) [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/#__codelineno-9-7) ### Africa [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/#__codelineno-9-8) [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/#__codelineno-9-9) Kenya::Nairobi [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/#__codelineno-9-10) [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/#__codelineno-9-11) ### North America [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/#__codelineno-9-12) [](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/#__codelineno-9-13) Canada::Ottawa`

卡片 `Kenya::Nairobi` 将会被附上 `Trivia > Capitals > Africa` 作为上下文标题而卡片 `Canada::Ottawa` 将会被附上 `Trivia > Capitals > North America` 作为上下文标题。

### 删除卡片[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/#_16 "Permanent link")

要删除一个卡片，只需删除复习规划标签和卡片相关文本。

### 忽略卡片[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/#_17 "Permanent link")

你可以使用诸如 `<!--Card text <!--SR:2021-08-20,13,290--> -->` 的HTML标签来将其从复习队列中移除。你可以随时移除该标签。

集中复习[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/#_18 "Permanent link")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

当前仅支持使用 集中复习此笔记中的卡片 命令。将复习所有卡组中来自该笔记的卡片。

数据统计[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/#_19 "Permanent link")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

统计页面可以使用 `View Statistics` 命令打开。

### 预估[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/#_20 "Permanent link")

计算将要到期的卡片数量。

![](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/st3v3nmw/obsidian-spaced-repetition/master/docs/media/en/stats_forecast.png)

### 复习间隔[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/#_21 "Permanent link")

统计卡片再次出现的时间间隔。

### 熟练度[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/#_22 "Permanent link")

统计卡片熟练度。

### 卡片类型[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/zh/flashcards/#_23 "Permanent link")

统计卡片类型：新卡片，较新卡片, 熟悉卡片（复习间隔超过一个月）。

回到页面顶部

---

# Obsidian Spaced Repetition

 

[Skip to content](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/#obsidian-spaced-repetition)

Obsidian Spaced Repetition[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/#obsidian-spaced-repetition "Permanent link")

=================================================================================================================================

![](https://img.shields.io/github/downloads/st3v3nmw/obsidian-spaced-repetition/total) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/downloads/st3v3nmw/obsidian-spaced-repetition/latest/total?style=flat-square) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/manifest-json/v/st3v3nmw/obsidian-spaced-repetition?style=flat-square)

Fight the forgetting curve by reviewing flashcards & notes using spaced repetition on Obsidian.md

Getting started

View the [quick demo](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/#quick-demo)
 below  
[Plugin installation](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/#installation)
  
General [guidelines & tips](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/resources/)
 about spaced repetition learning.

Features

[Flashcards](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/flashcards-overview/)
     [Notes](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/notes/)
  
[User Options](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/user-options/)
     [Commands](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/plugin-commands/)

* * *

[Repetition Algorithms](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/algorithms/)
     [Data Storage](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/data-storage/)

Help & Support

Visit the [discussions](https://github.com/st3v3nmw/obsidian-spaced-repetition/discussions/)
 section for Q&A help, feedback, and general discussion.  
Raise an issue [here](https://github.com/st3v3nmw/obsidian-spaced-repetition/issues/)
 if you have a feature request or a bug report.

Contributing

The plugin has been translated into over [10 languages](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/contributing/#translating)
 by the Obsidian community 😄. To help translate this plugin to your language, check the [translation guide here](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/contributing/#translating)
.  
Software developers can contribute [feature enhancements and bug fixes](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/contributing/#code)

* * *

Quick Demo[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/#quick-demo "Permanent link")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![user-interface-overview](https://github.com/user-attachments/assets/977bab30-cc5e-4b5c-849e-3881d82b3f8e)

1.  Display the [Note Review Queue](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/notes/#note-review-queue)
      
    
2.  Note review queue  
    
3.  Display the Obsidian command dialog to access the plugin [commands](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/plugin-commands/)
      
    
4.  `Flashcard Review Icon` Select a flashcard [deck](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/reviewing/#deck-selection)
     to [review](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/reviewing/#reviewing)
      
    
5.  Identify that flashcards within this note are in the `#flashcards/science/physics` [deck](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/decks/#using-obsidian-tags)
      
    
6.  A [single line question](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/flashcards/q-and-a-cards/#single-line-basic)
     (identified by the `::` separating the question and answer)  
    
7.  The plugin stores scheduling info within this [HTML comment](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/data-storage/#individual-markdown-files)
      
    
8.  `Spaced Repetition Status Area` The number of notes and flashcards currently due for review. Click to [open a note for review](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/notes/#selecting-a-note-for-review)
    .

* * *

Installation[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/#installation "Permanent link")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can easily install the plugin from Obsidian's community plugin section in the Obsidian app (Search for `Spaced Repetition`).

### Manual Installation[¶](https://stephenmwangi.com/obsidian-spaced-repetition/#manual-installation "Permanent link")

Advanced

Create an `obsidian-spaced-repetition` folder under `.obsidian/plugins` in your vault. Add the `main.js`, `manifest.json`, and the `styles.css` files from the [latest release](https://github.com/st3v3nmw/obsidian-spaced-repetition/releases)
 to the folder.

* * *
